Lu Gengquan vs. Tan Yuan Case: Continued Hearing 149

Originating from a Water Fee Issue

The Judge Advises Both Parties to Reconcile

Lu Gengquan, the owner of Lu Gengji Construction Company, previously sued Tan Yuan, a Cantonese architect of Hengyao Real Estate Company on Suzhou Road, for damaging his reputation. He hired lawyers Wu Kaisheng and Jiang Chiping to file a criminal self-accusation with the First Special District Court. Judge Zhan had summoned Tan once, but Tan did not appear, so a new date was set for another hearing. All details have been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday afternoon, the case reached the stage of continued hearing. The defendant, Tan Yuan, also arrived with his lawyer, Zhang Yuanmei. The plaintiff, Lu Gengquan, stated that the defendant fabricated rumors and, using his name, reported to the owner, Yu Jinjing, that the Jiangwan Zhengde Road buildings constructed by him required several hundred yuan for water connection fees from the Zhabei Water and Electricity Plant. This caused the owner to report to the Public Works Bureau, which sent a letter requesting an interview, considering that if it were true, his business license would be revoked. However, he actually never said such a thing; it was all fabricated by the defendant. Therefore, he filed a lawsuit to seek a legal resolution to restore his reputation. When questioned, the defendant Tan Yuan stated that he initially received Lu's report about the water connection fees, so he notified the owner. If there were fees, the owner and Lu would split them. Later, Lu wired back stating there were no fees, and he also reported this to the owner. Then, the owner Yu Jinyu testified that his Jiangwan Zhengde Road property was purchased from the Shanghai Bank. At that time, the bank had stated that if buildings were constructed, except for telephone and electric lights, all other expenses would be waived. Therefore, he advertised for bids and contracted with Lu Gengji Construction Company to start construction. Only because the area lacked tap water pipes, there was no tap water available, so they used river water for construction. He disliked the river water being unclean, so he ordered a temporary halt to construction, pending a request to the Water and Electricity Plant to install water pipes before resuming work. Therefore, he immediately consulted with both the plaintiff and defendant to discuss the water connection issue. At the time, Lu did not know if there would be special fees for water connection, so it was decided to discuss it further after inquiring. A few days later, he received a call from Tan Yuan, stating that he had received a report from Lu that 550 yuan was required for water connection fees, and he should split the cost with Lu. Upon hearing this, he immediately notified the Shanghai Bank and reported it to the Public Works Bureau for investigation. Unexpectedly, two days later, he received another call from Tan reporting that Lu had clarified that no fees were required for water connection, and he also stated this to the Shanghai Bank. At this point, the defendant's lawyer, Zhang Yuanmei, stood up and stated that the owner had intervened, stating that both parties were close friends and did not want to be involved in litigation for so long. It would be better to proceed with reconciliation, and the defendant was very willing to accept, but he did not know what the plaintiff's intentions were. Judge Zhan Liangce also stated that both the plaintiff and defendant were legitimate businessmen, and this matter only required clarifying the misunderstanding with the Public Works Bureau. If understanding was reached, the case could be dismissed. Therefore, he advised each to make concessions and discuss a reconciliation plan. The plaintiff's lawyers Wu and Jiang also indicated their agreement, stating that although this case was minor, it had major implications. Jiangwan Central District was currently planning to revive the market, and the municipal government had repeatedly announced that no illegal profiteering or extra demands were allowed. The sudden occurrence of this matter greatly impacted the future of the revival. Therefore, the Director of the Public Works Bureau must thoroughly investigate to clarify the truth. Now that the court had advised reconciliation, their client was very willing to accept, but the defendant must accompany the plaintiff and both lawyers to the Public Works Bureau to explain the misunderstanding and jointly publish a statement to restore their client's reputation. The court ordered the case to be adjourned to January 8th, 24th year [of the Republic], in the afternoon for further hearing, instructing both parties to attempt reconciliation.

Shen Ada Sues Fiancée for Fraud 150

Fiancée Claims Engagement Gifts Were Insufficient

And Wedding Date Was Missed, No One Came to Fetch Her

Yan Lianzhen, a female employee of the Maochang Air Conditioning Factory in Nanshi, was engaged to Shen Ada, also known as Shen Jichun, who resides at Wansheng Sesame Oil Shop on Seymour Road, in the 20th year of the Republic through the matchmaking of her brother-in-law Jin Youzhang and her sister Jin Yanshi. They have not yet married. Now Shen Ada has suddenly filed a criminal self-accusation with the First Special District Court, accusing Yan Lianzhen and Jin Youzhang and his wife of fraud. His reason is that he sent an engagement gift of 500 yuan when they were engaged and chose to marry in the 21st year of the Republic. Unexpectedly, after accepting the engagement, she made all kinds of demands, and when the wedding date arrived, the bride suddenly disappeared without a trace, causing the plaintiff to suffer losses. When negotiating with Jin and his wife, they said the bride could not be found as a way to evade responsibility, so it has been delayed until now. This situation is actually fraud, and he requests that the court punish them according to Article 363 of the Criminal Law and seeks compensation of 500 yuan for the engagement gift in an attached civil lawsuit. Yan Lianzhen's defense claims that when the engagement was set, it was stated that the engagement gift would be 400 yuan, four gold items, and four sets of clothing. They also agreed to complete the marriage in the spring of the 21st year of the Republic. However, the plaintiff only sent 200 yuan in engagement money and three gold items at the time and did not follow the original agreement. After repeated negotiations, they always made evasive promises. Moreover, the agreed-upon wedding date was missed, and no one came to fetch her, treating the marriage contract like a joke. Her reputation has been damaged, and the fault lies not with the defendant but with the plaintiff. Yesterday, Judge Huang Risheng of the First Special Court opened the Second Criminal Court for a hearing. Yan Lianzhen hired lawyer Yuan Yang'an for her defense. Judge Huang adjourned the case and instructed both parties to reconcile outside of court.

Xue Mailuo Law Firm Robbery Case: French Police File Appeal to the Third Instance 151

Requesting the Reversal of the Original Verdict and Remanding the Case for Retrial

On June 9th of this year, at around 4:00 PM, the Xue Mailuo Accounting Firm at No. 9 Edward Road in the French Concession was robbed of 12,000 yuan in cash. The suspects in the case, Zhang Zuming, Zhuang Jimeng, Wang Lianyou, and Tang Qingyue, were arrested by the French police and sent to the Second Special Court for trial. After being declared innocent, the Police Department, dissatisfied, filed an appeal with the Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. After the trial concluded, the appeal was rejected. All details and the judgments of the two trials have been reported in previous newspapers. However, the French Police Department was still unable to accept the third trial verdict and had submitted reasons, filing a third-instance appeal with the Supreme Court through the Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. The third-instance appeal statement of the French Police Department has been obtained and is transcribed below: "Regarding the matter of supplementing the reasons for the appeal, in the Zhang Zuming robbery case, the Jiangsu Shanghai Second Special District Court delivered a verdict of innocence, and the Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court rejected the appellant's appeal. The appellant then declared a third-instance appeal. All have been filed. The reasons for the appeal are hereby supplemented. The plaintiff in this case, Zhou Jinggeng, on June 9th of this year, at around 4:00 PM, dispatched Gao Yushu, Feng Tiyue, and Wan Guirong to the China Industrial Bank to exchange banknotes. Ten minutes after returning to the Xue Mailuo Accounting Firm at No. 9 Edward Road, they were robbed by four robbers armed with guns, who stole 12,000 yuan in banknotes. The fact that the robbery occurred has been thoroughly investigated and confirmed by the original trial. The only question to be studied is whether the appellees were the four robbers. During the robbery, the witnesses who saw the situation were Gao Yushu, Feng Tiyue, Wan Guirong, Qian Genghua, Mike Luo, and Wang Guixiang. At that time, none of the four robbers were captured. On June 17th, Zhang Zuming was first seen by Gao Yushu, who reported him to the police, who made the arrest. Although Feng Tiyue failed to identify him once at the Hongkou Police Station in the Public Concession, when Zhuang Jimeng and Wang Lianyou were subsequently arrested, Gao Yushu, Feng Tiyue, Wan Guirong, Qian Genghua, and Mike Luo were all able to point them out from the crowd. Finally, Tang Qingyue was apprehended, and all witnesses identified him in the first trial as one of the robbers. They all stated that Zhang Zuming and Wang Lianyou entered the office and ordered them not to move and not to look. They also searched Gao Yushu and Feng Tiyue and found banknotes. Zhuang Jimeng stood at the door on the second floor, and Tang Qingyue guarded the outer door. All four were carrying guns. The testimonies were consistent and without discrepancies. Wang Guixiang also identified Wang Lianyou in the second trial as the one who dragged him into the office, and Zhang Zuming held a gun to the manager, etc. Although his statement differed slightly from the previous five, he did identify Zhang Zuming and Wang Lianyou as the ones who committed the robbery by force and coercion. All the above witnesses had no feud with the appellees and had no reason to falsely accuse them. Zhang Zuming's confession at the Police Department was written by his own hand. His denials of the robbery in the second and third trials were clearly attempts to shirk responsibility. The Police Department did not threaten him before, during, or after he wrote his confession, nor did it interfere with his freedom. Zhang Zuming also showed no signs of injury. The original trial's statement that whether the confession was made of his own free will was not entirely beyond doubt seems somewhat arbitrary. Moreover, Zhang Zuming also confessed without reservation in the First Special District Court, where the trial was public, and there could not have been any possibility of coercion. As for the detective's instruction not to retract the confession, it was merely a fabrication by the appellee Zhang Zuming and is not credible. Since Zhang Zuming's confession was not obtained through improper means, it is only necessary to investigate whether it is consistent with the facts. The date, time, number of people, location, building, direction of the door, purpose of stealing money, and weapons used in his confession are all consistent with the eyewitness accounts of Gao Yushu and others. As for whether there was prior contact, it was not something the witnesses could have known. The original trial's finding that it was inconsistent with the facts is inappropriate. There is no doubt that Zhang Zuming was the perpetrator of the case. After Zhang Zuming confessed to Zhuang Jimeng, Wang Lianyou, and Tang Qingyue, Zhuang and Wang were first apprehended and sent to the French Concession Police Department, where they were identified by Feng Tiyue, Mike Luo, and others from the crowd. The original trial stated that after Zhuang Jimeng and Wang Lianyou were apprehended, Gao Yushu and the plaintiff Zhou Jinggeng's lawyer, Yan Luqing, had peeked into the trial room at the Hongkou Police Station beforehand, as stated in a letter from the Public Concession Police Department. However, whether the contents of the letter from the Public Concession Police Department are credible as evidence is questionable, and their description of their appearance is purely speculative. As for the defendants being suddenly arrested and appearing worried, which is inconsistent with the leisurely attitude of ordinary people, it seems unfounded. Zhuang Jimeng and Wang Lianyou were confessed by Zhang Zuming and identified by witnesses. Wang Lianyou entered to search, Zhuang Jimeng stood at the second door, and both were carrying guns. There is no doubt that they were the ones who committed the robbery. Tang Qingyue was also confessed by Zhang Zuming and identified by Gao Yushu and others after his arrest as the one who guarded the door and was carrying a gun. His crime has also been proven without doubt. Since there is direct and positive evidence of the crimes committed by the appellees, there is no need to study the appellees' rebuttals, and they cannot be used as the basis for the judgment. Therefore, this supplementary reason is filed, requesting the reversal of the original verdict and remanding the case for retrial. A fair judgment would be in the public interest. This appeal is respectfully submitted to the Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court for transmission to the Supreme Court for its consideration."

The Reason: At the time of the engagement, it was clearly stated that the engagement gift would be 400 yuan, four gold items, and four sets of clothing. It was also agreed to complete the marriage in the spring of the 21st year of the Republic. However, the plaintiff only sent 200 yuan in engagement money and three gold items at the time and did not follow the original agreement. After repeated negotiations, he always made evasive promises. Moreover, the agreed-upon wedding date was missed, and no one came to fetch her, treating the marriage contract like a joke. Her reputation has been damaged, and the fault lies not with the defendant but with the plaintiff. Yesterday, Judge Huang Risheng of the First Special Court opened the Second Criminal Court for a hearing. Yan Lianzhen hired lawyer Yuan Yang'an for her defense. Judge Huang adjourned the case and instructed both parties to reconcile outside of court.

Zhabei's Tight Winter Defense 152

Since the implementation of winter defense in this city from December 10th, lasting for three months until the end of February of the 24th year [of the Republic], it is learned that the heads of the two Public Security Bureaus of the New Zhabei Station, Gong Fengkui and Liang Fuchu, in addition to selectively increasing posts every day, also ordered patrolling police officers to accompany plainclothes detectives to inspect suspicious pedestrians in rotation. The security team patrols in shifts during the day and sends sentries to guard all strategic passes at night. The Bao'an Corps also assists the police and security team in making similar preparations at night, so petty thieves have no way to succeed, and theft cases seem to have decreased compared to the winter defense period last year.

The Domestically Built Fishing Vessel "Hai Kang" Achieves Excellent Results in Sea Trials 153

Traveling at 10.5 Nautical Miles per Hour

Already Submitted to the Ministry of Industries for Record-keeping

The Daily News reported that the Haili Fishing Vessel Bureau, a fishery organization in this city, noted that the trawlers used by Chinese fishermen for fishing were dilapidated and that the newly purchased fishing vessels were all dependent on foreign countries, resulting in a significant outflow of rights and interests. In order to reverse the losses, it started building a fishing vessel in May of this year by Hongxiangxing in Pudong. If it proved successful, it planned to continue manufacturing. It is learned that the fishing vessel has been completed. It is 135 feet long, has 600 horsepower, and the total cost is only 80,000 yuan. The internal equipment is the most modern of any trawler. After the vessel was completed, it was named "Hai Kang" and underwent sea trials outside Wusongkou the day before yesterday. The results were excellent, traveling at 10.5 nautical miles per hour. It has been submitted to the Ministry of Industries for record-keeping and will be used for fishing along the coast. It is planned to continue adding to the fleet in the future.

Harbor Quarantine Office Pays Attention to Livestock 155

No Harm to Human Health

Another Type of Pleuropneumonia Discovered

Foot-and-mouth disease has been discovered in livestock in this city. At the same time, the Veterinary Epidemic Prevention Institute has handled the inspection, and the import of foreign livestock has been temporarily suspended. The Datong News Agency reporter learned that since the discovery of the animal disease, the people of this city have been significantly affected. Therefore, the relevant parties were visited to investigate the situation, as follows:

Harbor Quarantine Office Attention 156

The Datong News Agency reporter visited Mr. Zhou Zhongqian, the secretary of the Harbor Quarantine Management Office at No. 2 Beijing Road, yesterday morning and learned that since the discovery of foot-and-mouth disease in livestock in this city, the office has paid great attention to imported livestock. According to Mr. Zhou, the transmission of foot-and-mouth disease is limited to cattle, pigs, sheep, etc., and there is no possibility of transmission to humans. Our health will not be affected.

Animal Diseases Harmful to Humans 157

Mr. Zhou continued, saying that the most severe animal epidemic is the plague, which is easily transmitted to humans, and the mortality rate is higher than that of rats. Rats infected with the plague are not necessarily dead, but humans infected with it have little hope of survival. However, the symptoms of the plague do not easily occur. According to the calculations of world veterinary experts, it generally occurs once every fifty years because its germs have a cyclical nature.

No Suitable Treatment Method 158

According to veterinary expert Sun Zhongqiu, the bacteria of foot-and-mouth disease (FOOT AND MOUTH DISHOSE) are commonly referred to as (GERM). Ten years ago, livestock in this city once had this disease. However, the famous veterinarians in Europe and the United States also feel helpless about the method of treating foot-and-mouth disease. The only method is the passive one, isolating the sick livestock, burning their excrement, washing the affected parts, etc. It is also said that the mortality rate of foot-and-mouth disease in livestock is not high. At most, two or three out of ten sick livestock die.

The Case of the Assassination of Tang Jiapeng Reopens Trial Yesterday 159

Wang Xinggao Denies Instructing the Murder; The Case Requires Investigation and the Hearing Was Adjourned

Tang Jiapeng, also known as A Yu, the former manager of the Great World Amusement Park, was shot and killed by a number of thugs instigated by an enemy at around 1:00 AM on June 18th of last year at the entrance of Great World as he was about to get into his car to go home. At the same time, Wu Xiancai, a bathhouse attendant from Yangzhou who was passing by, was killed by stray bullets. After the incident, detectives from the French Police Special Agency arrested the perpetrators Zhang Xiaosizi, also known as Zhang Tinggui, a native of Funing, and Zhao Guangfu, a native of Yangzhou, and confiscated a pistol and several bullets used by Zhao to kill Tang. They were sent to the Second Special Court and prosecuted for premeditated murder. After interrogation and judgment, Zhang was sentenced to 20 years of imprisonment and deprivation of civil rights for life.

Life Imprisonment 160

Deprivation of civil rights for life. The two criminals, dissatisfied, filed an appeal to the Third Branch of the High Court. As a result, the appeal was rejected. However, Zhao was still dissatisfied and has filed a third-instance appeal with the Supreme Court, which has not yet been decided. Zhang's sentence has been finalized and he has been sent to the Second Special District Prison to serve his sentence. Currently, Lang Bole, the Western Inspector of the Second Detective Team of the French Police Department, based on the confession of the arrested criminal Zhao Guangfu, learned that Wang Xinggao, a native of Funing residing at No. 46, Menggu Road, Zhabei (also known as Wang Xiaogao, 39 years old this year), was the mastermind behind the murder of Tang. At midnight on the 13th of this month, he took detectives Wang Rusong and Guo Shaorong, along with the Laozha Police Station, and dispatched detectives to Room 537 of the Central Hotel on Guangdong Road, arresting Wang and taking him back to the police station. He was sent to the Second Special Court the next day.

Interrogation and Detention for Investigation 161

All details have been reported in previous newspapers. The Police Department has requested and received approval from the court to transfer the two criminals Zhang Tinggui and Zhao Guangfu, who were previously apprehended, from the Second Special District Prison and the Detention Center to the Police Department for detention, confrontation with Wang, and thorough investigation. The investigation has now concluded. Yesterday morning at 10:00 AM, Judge Xiong Huiping and Secretary Tao Zongkan specially opened the Seventh Court for the trial. Wang's family and friends were all in court to listen, causing the courtroom to be overcrowded. Lawyer Gu Shouxi represented the Police Department in court. After the court opened, the judge ordered Wang Xinggao to be brought before the court. After questioning the defendant's age, place of origin, address, and occupation, Wang stated (age, residence, and place of origin omitted) that he is currently the warden of the First Prison in Wuchang, Hubei, and has never committed a crime before. Then the police lawyer stood up and stated

Prosecutorial Intent 162

And the details of the case and the investigation process of the Police Department, and stated that they are now prosecuting him for premeditated murder under Article 284 of the Criminal Law and requested the court to conduct the trial. The court verified the report and questioned Wang Xinggao about the assassination of Tang Jiapeng. Wang stated that he went to Hubei on August 1st of the 21st year of the Republic and was still there in the 22nd year, and had not returned to Shanghai. He himself is a civil servant, so how could he do such a murderous thing? He knows nothing about the assassination of Tang Jiapeng. In the 17th year of the Republic, he was a civil servant and the captain of the inspection team in the 26th Army, and he handled many murder and robbery cases in Zhabei, so he has many enemies. When he returned to Shanghai on July 28th of the lunar calendar last year, he was even rewarded by Chairman Chiang. He was also the head of the intelligence department in the 19th Army. Many bad people outside wanted to

Plot to Harm Me 163

He does not know Zhao Guangfu and asked for him to be brought up for questioning. At this point, the judge ordered the deputy chief detective of the Second Detective Team of the French Police Department in charge of this case to report on the investigation process. Then he ordered Zhao Guangfu to be brought to the court as a key witness. According to Zhao, Wang Xinggao instructed the assassination of Tang Jiapeng and was introduced to him by carpenter Zhou Er. In fact, he has always known Wang, but they do not greet each other often. At the time, carpenter Zhou Er told him that someone wanted revenge and that he would be given 100 yuan after it was done. First, he had tea with Zhou at the tiger stove on Hengfeng Road, and then a few more people came in. Zhou said they were all family members. Later, he did not hear them talking. Met Once 164

He had not met him after the assassination, and he had not received any money. It was now given to him by Sun Er. He does not know what revenge he was taking. He was confused for a moment and was fooled. If he had known that the law was so strict, he would rather beg for food than do it. The judge then questioned Wang Xinggao based on Zhao's confession. Wang stated that he was in Hubei at that time and there was no such thing. Zhao Guangfu had committed robbery and pawnshop fraud in Zhabei before, and he had handled his case. Zhao immediately said that there was no such thing and asked the court to investigate. He has no grudges with him at all. This time, while he was detained in the police station, he told him to speak with his conscience, and he was willing to support his elderly father. Speaking from the Conscience 165

Words should not be spoken carelessly. Regarding the case of Zhang Tinggui, whose official fate required a witness, it has now been confirmed that he has been brought to justice. The official also interrogated Liu Guogui, the disguised criminal, who testified that he was in the police station for six days and five nights, and heard Zhao Guangfu discussing with Wang Xinggao. Convention Procedures 170

The procedures for the Broadcast Celebration of the Victory Over the Bandits Convention have been promulgated by the Municipal Government and include eight articles: (1) In order to expand the celebration of the victory over the bandits, to make the public understand the tragedy of the bandit scourge, and to work together to thoroughly eliminate it, this government is specifically holding a Broadcast Celebration of the Victory Over the Bandits Convention in order to promote widespread publicity. (2) The Broadcast Celebration of the Victory Over the Bandits Convention will be hosted by the Shanghai Municipal Government and other relevant agencies. (3) The designated broadcasting station is the Shanghai Sino-Western Pharmacy Radio Station. (4) The broadcasting personnel will be invited by the Municipal Government by letter and divided into two parts: (A) speeches (each speaker's speech should be limited to fifteen minutes); (B) entertainment (each entertainment program should be limited to one hour). Recent News from Northern Steamers 177

Jingan Damaged Engine. The Jingan steamer of the Sanbei Company is currently sailing in North China. On the 24th of this month, the steamer departed from Tianjin, intending to go to Qingdao to load cargo and then return to Shanghai. When it sailed to a location twelve nautical miles off the coast of the Haihe River, the engine suddenly malfunctioned, rendering it unable to sail. The shipowner telegraphed the Tianjin branch to return to Tianjin. Yesterday, a telegram was received stating that it had been towed back to Tianjin on the 24th. The engine malfunction has now been repaired, and it is scheduled to depart from Tianjin again on the 27th to sail south.

Taishun Pipe Burst. The Taishun steamer of the China Merchants Bureau, on this trip from Shanghai to Tianjin, loaded a large amount of cargo from Shanghai. The steamer first went to Weihai and Yantai, but while en route, a water pipe inside the ship suddenly burst. A considerable amount of cargo in the cabin was damaged by the water leaking from the burst pipe. Fortunately, the burst water pipe was repaired by the shipowner. The damaged cargo will not be known until the ship arrives in Tianjin and is unloaded. The Bureau has informed the Tianjin branch by letter, and the branch will properly handle the matter of the damaged cargo.

Major Pharmaceutical Factories Agree on Cooperation Agreement for Common Injectable Drugs 178

A banquet was held yesterday to report the situation to various pharmacies.

The four pharmaceutical factories in this city, New Asia, Xinyi, Minsheng, and Haipu, are the largest in the domestic pharmaceutical industry. They produce more than a hundred kinds of drugs, which are suitable for the climate and physique of Chinese people, and their sales are quite wide. However, in recent years, the common injectable drugs produced by each factory have often fallen in price due to competition, sometimes even below cost. Therefore, they jointly negotiated and entered into a cooperation agreement to establish a unified price. Yesterday afternoon, a banquet was held at Jinlong Western Restaurant to invite various pharmacies in this city to report on the situation. Representatives from Sino-French, Sino-Western, Five Continents, Huayang, Jihuatang, Central, Xinhua, Taihe, Huamei, Dahua, Wanguo, Tianhua, Zhengwei, Dazhong, Tongfa, Huaying, Jicheng, Baohua, Nanyang, and other pharmacies attended. After the speech, Xu Xiaochu of Sino-French was publicly elected by the pharmacies to give a reply, stating that the success of this cooperation among the pharmaceutical factories was deeply commendable. This is not only a question between the new pharmaceutical industry and the new drug manufacturing industry, but also concerns the economy of the entire country. The pharmacy colleagues will naturally follow behind and support the success of the unified price. For a while, the cups clinked, and the banquet ended happily at 3 PM.

Shanghai Drug Rehabilitation Center Achieves Excellent Results, with 2,000 People Successfully Rehabilitated 179

Enthusiastic Enrollment, Municipal Government Decides to Establish Branch Centers

Since its establishment on June 15th of this year in Longhua, the Shanghai Municipal Temporary Drug Rehabilitation Center has, in six months, rehabilitated a total of 2,000 citizens, according to statistics. There are still many people who have registered but have not been admitted for rehabilitation. Therefore, the Municipal Government has ordered the Health Bureau to select suitable housing in Zhabei to continue establishing branch drug rehabilitation centers, which will soon be established. The details are recorded as follows:

Enthusiastic Enrollment 180

Since its establishment, the Municipal Temporary Drug Rehabilitation Center has seen very enthusiastic registration from citizens. Since its opening, more than 2,000 people have been rehabilitated. Later, due to the fixed number of 100 beds, and the fact that the Garrison Headquarters must send drug offenders every month, accounting for eight tenths of the beds, there were not many remaining beds. Citizens who wish to be rehabilitated must register in advance, and only when there are beds available can they be admitted for rehabilitation in order. Therefore, there are currently about 300 people who have registered and are waiting for rehabilitation.

Continuing to Establish Branch Centers 181

The Municipal Government, in view of the vast urban area and the considerable number of drug addicts, and the fact that the center's beds are insufficient, has ordered the Health Bureau to continue establishing branch centers in Zhabei. It is learned that the Health Bureau is looking for suitable housing and setting up 150 beds. The funding is currently in the budget, and it is expected to be established around next spring, which will undoubtedly benefit the citizens.

Simple Rehabilitation Method 182

As for the rehabilitation procedures, the center hires specialized doctors to use scientific acupuncture methods. The rehabilitation time for each person is about ten days. However, no substitutes are used, and no fees are charged. Therefore, from the time a person enters the center to the time of rehabilitation, the center needs to bear more than ten yuan per person. Based on the calculation of 300 people being rehabilitated per month, the expenses must total more than 3,000 yuan.

Spring and Autumn

Little West Heaven 198

— By Zhang Henshui

Chapter 7: Hearing Words, She Hides Her Tears and Sells Herself into Misery; Carefully Peeking at Invitation Cards, Eagerly Seeking Refuge.

When Li Shilian introduced the two Germans to Jia Duocai, his initial intention was simply to show off for his friend. He thought to himself that if Jia Duocai were to open a branch of his bank in Xi'an, there would certainly be times when he would need to utilize foreigners. Now that he had introduced them, in the future, if he thought of getting to know foreigners, it would be to my credit, and perhaps there would be times when he could help me. It was good to lay the groundwork now. Later, seeing that the Germans' attitude was not very good, and especially when they spoke about doing business, it was contrary to his original hope. He then felt a little sorry for Jia Duocai. Even though he didn't say anything, he could tell by his expression. So he smiled at him and said, "I didn't think they were doing business. If I had known they were like this, I wouldn't have introduced them." Jia Duocai smiled and said, "You look like you feel a little apologetic. What does it matter? Business may not succeed, but friendship remains. Moreover, the Construction Department is thinking of transferring a sum of money from our bank to buy some fuel oil trucks. Maybe they will buy them from these guys? In that case, we will have to deal with them anyway." When Li Shilian heard this, it was as if a firecracker had gone off behind his heels, and he was greatly surprised. He took Jia Duocai's hand and said, "What? Do you know the Director Gao here?" Jia Duocai said, "We bankers always have to deal with the officialdom. Meeting is friendship, not meeting is being strangers." Li Shilian said, "What do you mean by that?" Jia Duocai said, "I only go to see them when I have business. They are certainly willing to get close to people in the banking industry. Anyway, no one in the banking industry will borrow money from officials, so they can feel safe meeting with us." (100)

Three Wild Horses 199

— By Zhuo

Six leather shoes stepped on the cement sidewalk, one after another.

Three malnutritioned skinny faces secretly hid smiles.

Walk! Irregular steps moved us three lost souls. The yellow soup was just right, and the courage suddenly swelled so fat that we didn't put anyone in our eyes.

We, a group of three skinny guys, walked shoulder-to-shoulder on the sidewalk, singing "la la la" in our mouths. The women saw us and moved away from a distance. We laughed, and our hearts bloomed!

The neon lights shone high, and the five large characters of Sincere Co. and Qianli Xiang flowed with green and red light, illuminating people's faces red and green in the distance, changing color.

The snow scene in the large showcase made people feel strangely cold. The red-clothed old man smiled, and the wrinkles on his face were even deeper. But the white beard without a head or chin wouldn't make up its mind to shave once; it was like this last year, and it's still like this this year, fortunately the beard hasn't grown longer. Suddenly, I remembered that it was the old man's birthday today. Looking at his smiling vigor, carrying so many candies and pulling that little car, the old man really has his own interest.

On the other side, in a corner of the showcase, there were many gold-covered, silver-painted, embossed, and colorful New Year's cards. We remembered a couple who made a living in the education field in Changsha. Every year before Christmas, they sent a letter to congratulate the New Year, no, to report peace, implying that they had not starved to death or died of anger. But this year, there was no news. I took a cold breath and silently wished that all our partners were safe and didn't die quietly.

Looking at the showcase on the other side, there were many expensive cakes and candies. We swallowed a mouthful of saliva. Two partners turned their heads to look, smiling sympathetically. We touched the five small silver coins in our pockets. We still had to get through six days before payday! Watching the Western-dressed young man, carrying two girls and carrying large and small bags, smiling and turning into the carriage, with a few "pop" sounds, a burst of air was released from the butt, and it started! We didn't know who's anger we were taking, pulled two partners, and ran!

Like three wild horses released from their reins, taking advantage of the post-drinking exuberance, we galloped on our road.

Tidbits 200

— (Xuanzi)

The father complained to his son: "You buy a lot of lottery tickets every time, and they always seem to fall into the sea; you think there's only one in 500,000 chance, how can you get your share?"

The son said: "In this day and age, the hope of getting rich is very small. Except for this one in 500,000 chance, I'm afraid I don't even have a one in 50.5 million chance."

One Copper 201

— Zhou Xian

The way Mr. Yin's family spends money is worth noting.

Mr. Yin is quite a handsome Western-dressed young man. Mr. Yin has set foot in all fashionable places. In particular, he frequents dance halls at least three times a week. In such places, although one does not necessarily have to be lavish with money, one would at least not have to consider every single copper before spending it. However, Mr. Yin seemed somewhat special. He spent money very freely in entertainment venues, but he would always argue with rickshaw pullers over a single copper, not hesitating to fight to see whose strength was enough to overcome the other.

Mrs. Yin is a typical Shanghai housewife, taking going to the theater, riding in cars, and playing mahjong as her daily life, with playing mahjong as her second life. If she doesn't play mahjong for three days, she will feel uncomfortable. When she plays mahjong, she can play day and night, and she doesn't care about losing ten or twenty yuan. But she also has a special habit. In the vegetable market, she often argues with vegetable vendors over half a copper or a single copper, both sides blushing and cursing each other's ancestors and descendants.

Old Mrs. Yin, is Mr. Yin's mother, and also Mrs. Yin's mother-in-law, is a kind-faced, vegetarian Buddhist old lady. This old lady goes to Hangzhou every year to burn incense, and she doesn't care about spending one or two hundred yuan. In addition, she is always generous in donating money to repair bridges, build roads, and build pagodas and temples. Therefore, monks, nuns, and Taoists who come to solicit donations with alms books always receive three or five yuan from Old Mrs. Yin. However, yesterday this old lady ordered a maid to buy incense sticks, and the maid pocketed one copper in change, which was discovered by the old lady, who then scolded her severely. Moreover, this morning, she forced the maid to pack her bags and get out.

Record of Fragrant Mist 202

— Originally written by Princess Der Ling of the Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

Because if you shake it too quickly or not carefully enough, often several sticks will fall out at the same time: this is considered a warning that the person's faith is not firm, and it is very unfavorable for their own or their family's illness, and they must shake it again. Sometimes, if you shake it too quickly, all the sticks may fall out together, which means that the deity is saying that the illness is incurable. Therefore, everyone is very careful when shaking the divination tube: if you encounter an enthusiastic temple keeper, they will also guide you from the side, so you can't help but give them some incense money! After shaking for a while, inevitably one stick will fall out alone, which is considered the indication from the deity in the dark. Then, the person seeking the divination carefully looks at the number on the stick, tells the temple keeper, and the temple keeper finds the divine prescription for them according to this number. The so-called divine prescription is the same as the divination verses we can see in various temples now, which are narrow and thin strips of yellow paper printed with a dozen or so kinds of medicine names: usually, a stack is strung together with thread and hung on the wall in order, and when needed, you only need to recognize the number and pull one off.

After the patient or the patient's family obtains the divine prescription, they naturally dare not delay, and rush to the pharmacy, mostly to the pharmacy closest to the temple. Nineteen out of ten of these pharmacies get their business from the temple, and the shop owner, out of gratitude, cannot help but reward the temple's manager or temple keeper. They purchase the medicine according to the prescription; fortunately, the medicine prescribed on these divine prescriptions is mostly mild and weak, and after the patient drinks it, even if it is not effective, in any case, it will definitely not immediately lead to death. So, divine prescriptions usually don't cause trouble! (210)

Silver Chamber Pot 203

— Chi Fo

Indeed, geographers say, "The civilization and barbarism of a country depend entirely on the length of its coastline." Because a long coastline makes transportation convenient and cultural infusion easier; a short coastline obstructs transportation, and natural evolution is difficult. For example, countries such as England, Japan, Germany, and France have long coastlines and naturally become civilized countries; Congo and Uruguay, located in the interior of Africa, are naturally always barbaric nations. This is the geographer's well-reasoned proof.

But, we believe that "the civilization and barbarism of a country depend entirely on the number of chamber pots." Our reasoning is even more sufficient than that of geographers. Why? For example, friends who live in Western-style houses are naturally "civilized classes." They have flush toilets and porcelain chamber pots. Naturally, it is not appropriate to display chamber pots at the entrance of mansions and Western-style houses, let alone display domestic chamber pots. But when you get to the interior, with its rows of pit latrines and checkerboards of chamber pots, can't you use this to measure the civilization or barbarism of the area? Go further into the interior. You can meet chamber pots everywhere, round, square, long, oval, enough to be experimental teaching materials for geometry teachers. Porcelain, mud, coarse, fine, light-colored, purple sand, enough to see the development of our country's porcelain industry. We only need to appreciate the colorful chamber pots squatting next to the pit latrines, and without your investigation, you can know the civilization or barbarism of this place.

I don't know which Fenghua man invented a silver chamber pot to make his woman happy, making it a necessary item for the bride's dowry. If this treasure is not in the trousseau, it is not considered a good trousseau. The whole body of this silver chamber pot is oblate; there is a mouth on it, about only an inch and a half in diameter, and the circumference is four inches and six points. Such precise calculations, but raise a serious question. Because this treasure is shared by men and women: men of course have no problem, but for women, we admire their "perfect proportions."

Little Recipes

Winter Home-Style Vegetables 204

— Sha Yu

Time flies like an arrow, and in the blink of an eye, the winter solstice has passed again; the north wind howls, the New Year's drums sound, and another year quickly passes. The year is so desolate, and all industries are so withered, yet a year's time passes like relentlessly flowing water. In these rich people's homes, the radiators are already warmly radiating heat, and the dogs kindly urge donations for disaster relief, and the donations have already reached a certain amount; soup kitchens have been opened, and porridge factories have also opened their doors. With a bowl of porridge and a bowl of rice, ordinary people can also strengthen their meals and eat more, without worrying about hunger. Sha Yu dares not say "rejoice in the joy of the world before others," but talking about recipes while basking in the sun or chatting around the stove is also a timely and beautiful thing, especially when it comes to home-style vegetables.

Biting on Vegetable Roots

"Warm clothes and a full stomach of vegetable rice"; "If you can bite on vegetable roots, there is nothing in the world you cannot do," which shows that there is a lot to say about a single vegetable root! Winter is the season for vegetables, which can be roughly divided into five kinds: green vegetables, cabbage, spinach, shepherd's purse, and yellow sprouts. Winter green vegetables are large, plump, and green, stimulating the appetite. Green vegetables, whether cooked plain or with meat, are sweet and delicious. Cooking porridge or rice with rice is fragrant and has a unique flavor. Two bowls of vegetable rice and a serving of cooked meat, basking in the sun and eating slowly, that kind of fragrant, sweet, and delicious taste is truly endless. Long-stemmed green vegetables, pickled, when they are just ripe, the color is tender yellow and translucent, and the taste is slightly sour, tender, and fresh, truly a good vegetable to eat with porridge.

The "braised stew" in Suzhou restaurants is a unique and successful delicacy; the dish is cabbage cooked with shredded pork, but it is fatty, crisp, and tender. When you eat it in your mouth, it is very tasty. The cabbage in the dish is stewed until it is so soft that it melts in your mouth, truly extraordinary. Cabbage and chili peppers pickled raw are spicy and refreshing, and can be eaten with porridge or to sober up.

Although shepherd's purse is a wild plant, it can be served at banquets and made into delicacies; stir-frying it with winter bamboo shoots is an excellent vegetarian dish in winter. Stir-frying it with chicken slices or shredded pork is also very tasty. Shepherd's purse and shredded pork can also be wrapped into "spring rolls," which are also exquisite snacks of the season!

Yellow sprouts are the most tasteless of vegetables, but they are the cheapest. Cooking them with chili sauce is quite good for eating rice, and is indeed an economical vegetarian dish for ordinary people.

Snow in Red and Radish

In addition to the five kinds of vegetables, "snow in red" and "radish" also have a considerable place in winter vegetables. The shape of snow in red is similar to green vegetables, but the stems are thin and round, and the leaves are also hairy like bird feathers; snow in red has a spicy taste when raw, and must be pickled first to remove the spicy taste before it can be eaten. The newly pickled snow in red has a color like emerald, clear and bright. When you bite it in your mouth, it is tender and fresh, and the deliciousness of the sweat cannot be described in words, truly the best vegetable to eat with porridge. Newly pickled snow in red, stir-fried or cooked in soup, is suitable for both meat and vegetarian dishes, such as snow in red stir-fried with winter bamboo shoots, and snow in red cooked with fish fillet soup, which are all seasonal delicacies at banquets.

"Taihu radish" is as plump and tender as a pear these days. While eating hot pot, it is easy to cause throat problems, and raw radish is a symptomatic remedy for throat problems. Stewing raw radish with rock sugar is also a wonderful prescription for treating coughs. Radish cut into shreds and mixed raw, or cooked with salted meat, are all very good home-style dishes.

There is a side dish in temples called "old age," which is made by slightly pickling ginseng radish, then cutting it into small pieces with orange peel and green vegetables, stuffing it into a jar, and eating it about a month later. It tastes crispy and fragrant, and is very good for drinking wine.

In this winter dusk after a year of hard work, Yang Hui had already said: "At the end of the year, the wax sacrifices, cooking sheep and roasting lambs, drink wine to reward yourself." Winter is a time for enjoyment in life. Pigs have been raised fat, fish are also large and unparalleled, and even chickens and ducks are full of feathers, fat, and edible. Large pieces of meat, large strips of fish, as long as you have money, you can eat endlessly, but the year is so bleak, and under the drought, finding a vegetable root is already supreme happiness, and those vegetable roots are probably nowhere to be found! The north wind is gradually strong, and I sincerely hope that people who gather around the stove to keep warm and drink wine to reward themselves will remember the disaster victims struggling with hunger and cold, slightly restrain their appetites, and do a little good deed. That is the supreme merit! Immeasurable merit!

Watch Tomorrow Afternoon's Battle Against Jinan—

The Datong University Yixing Fellow Villagers Association, in order to relieve the drought disaster in their hometown, took advantage of the opportunity of the Central National Martial Arts Sports College basketball team's visit to Shanghai to continue holding disaster relief basketball games. Datong was more accurate in shooting, and won 42 to 39. In the second game, the National Sports College played against the East Asia Sports College. The National Sports College, with its well-practiced passing and magical shooting, was difficult to grasp. As a result, East Asia lost 24 to 64. The general situation of the two games is as follows:

Datong Wins Nanxing

42 to 39

Datong's basketball skills have improved a lot. At the beginning of the game, the three forwards scored in succession, taking the lead with 6 to 0, with great momentum. Nanxing was not willing to be outdone, and Liu Daqi scored under the basket, tying the score. After that, the scores were very close. Datong always led. The result of the first half was 20 to 18, Datong won.

In the second half, Datong continued to gain momentum. Shanghai Municipal First Stadium Table Tennis Tournament 209

Public Donation Receipts for Viewing the Finals

The Shanghai Municipal First Stadium, yesterday, entrusted by the Shanghai Municipal General Donation Committee for Disaster Areas, issued a notice to solicit donations for disaster relief. It stipulates that anyone who generously donates before 8 PM on the 31st of this month can use the donation receipt to watch the table tennis competition at the stadium. On the afternoon of the 31st of this month, at 8 PM, the match between the Guangdong team and the Langya team will take place. The skills of these two teams are well recognized by the people of Shanghai. Donating money can not only benefit the disaster victims but also allow one to watch an exciting table tennis match, which is truly a win-win situation. The method is that a receipt for two jiao (small silver coins) allows two people to watch, and so on. However, members participating in this table tennis competition can hold two two-jiao (small silver coins) receipts per team, allowing ten players to enter the stadium to watch (teams disqualified from the competition are not included in this rule). The donation collection point is the stadium office, and receipts will be given upon collection. The back of the receipt will be stamped with the Shanghai Municipal First Stadium logo. Receipts without the logo are not receipts raised by the stadium and cannot be used for entry.

Educational News

The Nurses' Education Committee Held Its First Meeting Yesterday 211

Curriculum Standards Equipment Standards

Resolutions Passed on Filing and Examinations

(Nanjing, 26th) The Nurses' Education Committee held its first meeting on the 25th. Chairman Gu Shusen reported on the establishment process and resolved: (1) To elect Gu Shusen as the chairman of the committee. (2) To revise and approve the rules of procedure for the meeting. (3) Matters resolved by the Chinese Nurses' Association presented to the congress will be incorporated into the committee's proposals for discussion. If there are matters not covered by the committee's proposals, they will be raised for discussion separately. (4) In accordance with the regulations for vocational schools, the entry qualifications for senior vocational schools (junior high school graduation) and the three-year study period were set, as well as the required courses and minimum equipment standards for nursing schools. The method is to use the Chinese Nurses' Association's original survey of the general situation of nursing school courses as reference material and entrust Pan Jingzhi, Shi Xien, Liu Ganqing, Hu Dun, and Zhu Bihui to draft and submit it for approval at the next meeting, and then announce it. (5) After the curriculum and equipment standards are announced, the filing of nursing schools will begin, and the filing procedures must be completed by the end of July of the 25th year. The investigation form will be drafted simultaneously by the curriculum and equipment committee and submitted for discussion at the next meeting. (6) The Chinese Nurses' Association will continue to conduct the nursing school examinations in accordance with previous methods until the filing procedures are completed. (7) The training of nursing school teachers should be planned and organized by the central government. Before the central government determines the method, provincial and municipal nursing schools with good performance that have been filed may run teacher training classes, but they must report for record. (8) The second meeting is scheduled to open at 10 AM on the 28th.

The Ministry of Education Orders Shanghai Vocational Schools to Strive to Install Military Training Equipment 212

(Nanjing, 26th, Special Dispatch) The Ministry of Education ordered the principals of public and private schools in Shanghai lacking military equipment above the vocational level, stating that it has approved the Training Supervision Department's consultation. According to the report by Pan Youqiang, Director of the National Military Education Department, who went to Shanghai to inspect the military training equipment of various schools, except for the Merchant Marine School and Fudan University, the other schools were either incomplete or completely lacking. A list of the names and quantities of military equipment lacking in various schools in Shanghai was attached to the Ministry. It is important to check the military training equipment. The Ministry previously sent a letter to the Training Supervision Department requesting that the necessary equipment for military training be determined and the minimum equipment standards be set. The Training Supervision Department has since determined and sent the standards, which the Ministry has ordered to be purchased in full last year. The equipment cost is 1,043.8 yuan for schools above the vocational level and 513.8 yuan for high schools. The quantity and price of the items have been listed in detail. The amount is not too much. Even if the school's funds are tight, it can still be set up with effort. The original list is hereby issued and ordered to handle the missing quantities separately.

Ministry of Education Section Chief Dai Investigates the Cause of Student Suicide at Zhongnan School 219

Moral Education Should Focus on Individuality and Not Involve Kneeling or Slapping Hands

Wang Bonian, a third-year junior high school student at the private Zhongnan Middle School in this city, committed suicide by hanging himself on the 3rd of this month. The Ministry of Education sent Section Chief Dai Yingguan to investigate the truth. After investigating the cause of death, the only evidence was two letters left to his brother Wang Songnian and the school's moral education director Teng. After carefully reviewing the words in the letters, it is not difficult to infer the reason for his suicide. The first statement clarified that in view of the imminent demise of the country, he did not want to be a subjugated slave and die in humiliation in the future. Second, it was not caused by shame and anger from being subjected to a deserved punishment (i.e., kneeling), and it was actually not related to Director Teng. Third, please ask the school to quickly resolve a certain problem in the third grade (i.e., the problem with a certain physics teacher). Fourth, please ask his brother to take good care of his mother, and the school to treat his brother well. The student had a quiet personality and excellent academic performance, but his family was poor. Director Teng usually treated him quite well. Later, the student was dissatisfied with the physics teacher's lecture, and his attitude was slightly inappropriate. Director Teng ordered him to kneel for a long time. The student cried bitterly while kneeling. After returning home, he was unusually depressed and committed suicide the next day. His pessimism had been around for a long time, and a moment of shame and anger made him not want to live anymore. Therefore, the school is not legally responsible for the student's death. However, from the perspective of education, kneeling as a form of humiliation is not a proper method of punishment. It is reported that the Ministry of Education has ordered the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau to warn the school and instructed all schools to pay attention to observing the personality of students in moral education in the future, provide good guidance, and not to engage in improper punishments such as kneeling and slapping hands.

Hangzhou High School Invites Ma Yinchu to Lecture 220

Zhejiang Provincial Hangzhou High School invited domestic economics expert Dr. Ma Yinchu to the school to give a lecture during the memorial week the day before yesterday. After being introduced by Principal Xiang of the school, Mr. Ma stepped onto the stage amid applause and gave a lecture entitled "The Silver Problem." Based on his experience and far-sighted vision, Mr. Ma elaborated that the United States' increase in silver prices had a great impact on our country, but the Japanese took the opportunity to profit by exporting from Dalian and Hong Kong to the United States to buy cotton, weave cotton cloth, and dump it in China. He also used alerting words to awaken the youth, saying that this is a national and ethnic problem as a whole, not just a local problem of silver. The listeners were all inspired.

Shanghai Suburban Improvement Zone of the Vocational Education Society Held Its Supplementary Opening Ceremony Yesterday 221

After the six-year trial of the Xugongqiao Improvement Association was completed, the China Vocational Education Society moved its human and financial resources to the new county of Shanghai to organize the Shanghai suburban rural improvement zone, dividing Wu Jiaxiang and other three places into improvement associations, starting with three different methods. The opening ceremony was held yesterday (the 25th). In the morning, we visited the achievement exhibition and the village situation. The opening ceremony was held at 1 PM. The details are as follows:

Participants 222

On this day, in addition to Huang Renzhi, Jiang Wenyu, Yang Weiyu, Yao Huiquan, Shi She and others from the China Vocational Education Society, there were also Shanghai County Mayor Pan Zhongjia, Zhang Jingye from the county party headquarters, Zhu Hange, director of the county education bureau, Wang Kuizheng from the Gaoqiao Rural Improvement Association, Lu Yimin from the Provincial Yutang Public Education Center, Zhang Yi from the County Agricultural Education Center, Tao Xiaodong from the Guangci Orphanage, Wang Yinfo from the Caohejing Agricultural Group, and local gentry Huang Zaishu, Li Hengzhai, Wu Jingqing, and no less than thousands of farmers from the entire district.

A Glimpse of the Village 223

The district began preparations in March of this year and was officially established on July 1st. The trial period is set for three years. An office is set up in Zhao Jiatang. The entire district is about 20 square miles, with 408 households and 1,798 people. In terms of education, Hongying Elementary School is established, and compulsory public education is actively promoted, with 335 male and female students. Three public education centers have also been established, with academic lectures, science competitions, improved marriages, educational investigation mobile education groups, and public education boards. In terms of agriculture, a farmers' lending office has been established, and the establishment of a production cooperative, a central farm, and the promotion of tree planting, bamboo planting, fish farming, and pig farming are being planned. In terms of construction, a work-rest bell is set up, and a construction engineering committee is established. In terms of security, one clinic and four simple pharmacies are set up, a census is conducted, and security groups are established. The gambling style has automatically disappeared, and the village appearance is very clean.

Shandong Social Education Delegation Comes to Shanghai to Investigate Social Education Situation 228

A Group of Fifty-Four People Visits Shanghai for Three Days

Visit to the Municipal Education Bureau and Other Institutions Today

The social education delegation, jointly organized by the principals of public education centers in various counties of Shandong Province and the social education service personnel training class, came to Shanghai the day before yesterday to investigate the social education situation in this city. The group consists of a total of 54 people. The members of the delegation and the itinerary are listed as follows:

The delegation is organized by the graduates of this year's Shandong Provincial Social Service Personnel Training Class. The leader of the delegation is Zhang Xuechun, the deputy leader is Wang Dian, and the instructor is Yang Xiangjiu. It is divided into five groups, with one group leader for each group. In addition to the students of the class, there are also the fifth section chiefs of the governments of Ling County, Gaomi, Jimo, etc., the director of the Guantao Public Education Center, the superintendent of Putai County, and the director of the Lijin County Normal School, totaling 54 people.

The delegation departed on the 13th of this month and visited the Rural Construction Research Institute in Zouping, the Zouping Experimental County Government, the Sunjiazhen Cotton and Mulberry Cooperative, and the village primary school. In Nanjing, they visited the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, the Capital Public Education Center, the Public Education Experimental Zone, the Municipal Library, the Public School, the Public Sports Field, the Central University Experimental School, the Jinling University Agricultural College, the Santiao Lane Primary School, and the Ordnance Factory Children's School. In Qixia Mountain, they visited the Rural Normal School. In Zhenjiang, they visited the Provincial Education Department, the Zhenjiang Normal School, and the Zhenjiang Public Education Center. In Wuxi, they visited the Provincial Education College, the Huibei and Beixia Experimental Zones, the Experimental People's School, and the Experimental Public Education Center.

The itinerary for the visit to Shanghai on the day before yesterday was to visit the museum, the newspaper, the YMCA, and the National Goods Market yesterday. Today, they will visit the Municipal Government, the Municipal Education Bureau, the Municipal Public Education Center, the Municipal Zoo, the Shanghai Industrial School, and the primary schools in various districts. Tomorrow, they will visit the China Vocational School, the Shanghai Middle School Experimental Primary School, etc., and then take a car back to Jinan tomorrow afternoon.

Local impressions: According to Mr. Zhang Xuechun, the leader of the delegation, who spoke to the Shanghai social reporter yesterday, the goal of this southern visit is mainly social education, with a secondary focus on primary school education. In Nanjing, the Ordnance Factory Workers' Children's School and the teachers and students of the whole school are completely workers. The Santiao Lane Primary School is a rural school in the city, and they all have a spirit of hard work. In addition, the Qixia Mountain Rural Normal School is integrated with the village, and the results are very good. In Shanghai, the important goal is to visit social education institutions.

Shandong Social Education: According to Zhang, the leader of the delegation, the goal of the education sector in Shandong Province is to focus on the implementation of social education. The establishment of a training class for social education service personnel is to supply talents. However, the social education fee in Shandong Province is quite small, with an average of only four or five thousand yuan per county per year. Recently, the director of the Shandong Education Department advocated survival education, so that social education and school education are integrated. It is currently being planned for implementation.

Fourteenth Anniversary of Liangjiang 230

Liangjiang Girls' School held its fourteenth-anniversary celebration and carnival the day before yesterday. The auditorium was decorated with a completely new look, and the Party and national flags were hung with cypress branches in front of the gate. After eight o'clock, representatives of various organizations and ordinary guests arrived one after another and gathered in the large playground to review the Boy Scouts. At ten o'clock, they entered the auditorium in an orderly manner to hold the anniversary ceremony. Principal Lu Qiaoyun presided over the meeting, and the emcee was Qiaoyun Sun. First, the chairman delivered an opening speech, briefly stating that the school was established in the ninth year of the Republic of China and has a history of fourteen years. In the past, due to financial difficulties, there were many twists and turns. Fortunately, the faculty, staff, and students cooperated sincerely and wholeheartedly to achieve the considerable scale of today. At present, various facilities are gradually being completed, and other buildings that have not yet been built are still in the planning stage. It is hoped that the entire project can be completed by the fifteenth anniversary next year. Next, representatives of the faculty and staff, Dean Zhang Yuansheng, representatives of alumni, and representatives of students delivered speeches successively. Finally, the guests gave speeches, unanimously expressing their admiration for Principal Lu's hard work and the spirit of cooperation between teachers and students, and praising the seriousness of the school's management and the completeness of its facilities. Then, the chairman gave a thank you speech and the meeting was dismissed with music. Starting at two o'clock in the afternoon, a carnival performance was held. Guests who had not been able to arrive in the morning arrived in the afternoon, making the crowd even larger. On that day, the performers included the roles in the new dramas "A Piece of Patriotic Heart" and "Two Women of Different Eras," which were played by students from different provinces of the school, each with its own unique flavor and quite interesting. Other performances included piano, harmonica, chorus, Beijing opera, and single-knife martial arts by alumna Zhai Lianyuan. The flying fork martial arts by the guests from the Chinese Athletic Association were also extremely exciting and won a lot of enthusiastic applause. It was reported that there were more than ten other programs such as dramas like "Zhuo Wenjun," "After Returning Home," "Learning Mandarin," and "Electric Baton," which were originally planned to continue performing at the teachers' and students' party at 7:30 that evening. Unexpectedly, foreign guests broke into the school, directly disrupting the order, and the performance was stopped immediately. The students' family members, relatives, schoolmates, and friends who had already arrived were greatly disappointed, and the school students expressed their deep apologies to the long-waiting guests.

Student National Products Year's Wishes 232

The year of the Republic of China, full of vitality and activity, has been designated by the people of Shanghai and various organizations as the Student National Products Year. Sending Off the Women's National Products Year 234

— Yang Dehui

Time flies like an arrow, and the vigorous Women's National Products Year has passed with time and become a historical relic. We silently observe the achievements of the past year, which makes people feel unspeakably sad. According to reports, in the eleven months of the country, women's cosmetics and clothing supplies amounted to more than two million yuan, and what is even more shocking is that in this amount of two million yuan, Shanghai accounted for more than three-quarters, totaling 1.6 million yuan. The Women's National Products Year, initiated by the women's community in Shanghai, has such a huge amount of consumption, and this contradictory behavior is worthy of people's criticism.

However, we cannot blame the enthusiastic women who initiated it. They have certainly done their duty to promote national products, but who would have expected the achievements of the past year to be like this? I am afraid that it was not expected by the enthusiastic women in the first place?

We should treat the past as if it were dead. For the future, we hope that women, especially women in Shanghai, will turn over a new leaf. It is not impossible to "know the times and be a hero." Of course, love of beauty is inherent in human beings, but it should be done under the principle of promoting national products!

Finally, the Women's National Products Year has passed. Women should not regard the end of the Women's National Products Year as the end of their responsibility. They should catch up quickly to recover huge economic interests for the country. I respectfully use this article to bid farewell to the Women's National Products Year.

Women Should Always Be Responsible for Using National Products 235

— Yan Boshou

This year's Women's National Products Year is at the end of its strength. In the blink of an eye, it will be parting ways with us! On the track of advancing time, the five characters "Student National Products Year" have already been written in large letters, which clearly shows the great and unyielding expression of those who promote national products. This year's failure will still reap the success of next year.

But what we need to know is where is the cause of the failure of the "Women's National Products Year"? In a nutshell, it is because women have not worked hard and pooled their efforts. Especially some young ladies and wives have forgotten their responsibilities.
