During the Student National Products Year, Production and Sales Should Pay Attention to the Needs of Students 236

— Tian Xi

The year of the Republic of China is called the "Student National Products Year." During the Student National Products Year, I think that both the production and sales of national products should pay attention to the needs of students.

What do students need? In the first semester of the 23rd year, the Education Bureau had already told the public that from this year onwards, students must wear uniforms uniformly. This is not only a large outlet for domestic woolen cloth, but also essential for the related parts. For example, Boy Scouts' black turn-down woolen socks, with each person buying two pairs, is also a not-small business. However, when I went to buy those woolen socks for my young child, I ran into many stores with sock factory signs, but when I arrived at the company specializing in national products, I couldn't find the prescribed socks. I asked the sales staff why they didn't have black ones. Their replies were mostly: "The factory doesn't make that kind of product, so we don't have it for the market." I told them that there is such a need now, and that both junior high school boys and girls have to receive Boy Scout training, so they can order from the factory, and there will definitely be sales. The above fact tells us that both the production and sales parties have not paid attention to the needs of the market. I think that the store's purchasing staff and the factory's designers should pay attention to educational news when reading the newspaper, which may be relevant and beneficial to their business.

After knowing the needs of the market, if there are items that we do not have in our national products, we can also discover the possibility of imitation. For example, Boy Scouts need to wear small knives. It is said that there are no national products for those small knives. Instead of secretly competing with your peers to manufacture the same goods, why not open up new paths? University students and middle school students all need safety razors, and junior high school students need Boy Scout knives. Please pay attention to the production and sales parties and supply them.

The production and sales parties should have the greatest cooperation and jointly seek a way out for national products. This is a major event that has not yet been fully achieved. In the "Winter Solstice Gift" window, the largest bookstore displays Western-style letter paper and envelopes in brocade boxes, as if domestic letter paper and envelopes are not suitable for exhibition! In the "Student National Products Year" of the Republic of China, I hope that the bookstores and stationery stores that sell exercise books will all use domestic paper to make them, cooperating sincerely with the production party. If there are really students who are willing to buy foreign goods, because they are all buying domestic products anyway, they will use them even if they don't want to.

To be honest, let me end this article. The above is the feeling caused by going to buy Boy Scout socks for my young child on the road.

Contribution to Chairman Chiang 237

— Wang Shouqiu

Recently, when Chairman Chiang left Nanjing, he issued a handwritten order, instructing the Nanjing Municipal Government to promote national products, stating that "the general public has a tendency to be extravagant, and they cannot be satisfied with anything other than foreign goods, which has led to the decline of domestic industries and an increase in the annual trade deficit. If we do not strictly correct this and actively promote the use of domestic products, how can we achieve national prosperity and national rejuvenation? In the future, we must order the general public, regardless of poverty, to use domestic products as the main priority, in order to cultivate the patriotic concept of the entire people and block the huge annual outflow." This is indeed a very important issue, and we can certainly understand Chairman Chiang's intention. However, promoting national products is not just a matter for Nanjing, so I think Chairman Chiang should extend it to all officials across the country to implement the use of national products. Now, I would like to contribute a few suggestions for Chairman Chiang and Mayor Shi of Nanjing to adopt.

First, I think Chairman Chiang should order all agencies across the country that people who wear foreign clothes are not allowed to enter the office to work, are not allowed to participate in any meetings, are not allowed to attend commemorative weeks, and are not allowed to visit their superiors. Those who violate the rules will be given a demerit for the first time, a fine for the second time, and dismissed for the third time.

Second, all public goods must not be purchased from foreign countries. Those that must be purchased from foreign countries (limited to those with no domestic substitutes) must first be submitted to the relevant superiors for approval.

Third, each agency should elect impartial staff to form a national products review committee to carefully review the goods purchased by each agency. If there are any doubts or proof that they are not domestic products, they may submit a request to the competent authority to order the general affairs to replace them.

Fourth, the original foreign goods in each agency should be certified by the national products review committee, listed and filed for future reference, and no more foreign goods can be purchased in the future. If foreign goods are found in the future, the national products review committee shall be jointly responsible.

If we can do this, I think promoting national products will definitely have a great effect!

Introduction to Domestic Silk Floss 238

— Zhu Weixuan

The climate is getting colder with the wheels of time! The issue of winter warmth is urgently needed to be resolved. The general people in the current society mostly use woolen fabrics for winter clothing, which is neither economical nor practical, and most woolen fabrics are foreign goods, which invisibly creates a shocking huge trade deficit! I believe that domestic silk floss can at least replace some of the need for woolen fabrics. Anyone who has used silk floss admits that silk floss is light, soft, and warm, and it is indeed the only wonderful product for winter warmth!

Cocoons are the raw material for making silk floss; however, even cocoons made by the same silkworm are of varying quality. Double palace cocoons are white and tough, and are the highest quality of silk floss. The lowest quality is silk floss made from thin-skinned cocoons, which is dull in color, brittle in nature, and much less effective!

Silk floss is originally a sideline of farmers in western Zhejiang. The annual output is more than 10,000 dan, worth more than 3 million yuan. The best quality is produced in Huzhou and Yuhang. Every year, a considerable amount is transported and sold to other places.

The function of silk floss, whether for lining clothes or lining quilts, is extremely light, soft, and warm, and even if it is old and knotted, it can be light and warm as new after being re-lined. It is both practical and economical, so some people are increasing its use. However, in Shanghai, there are many counterfeit and inferior silk flosses, and it is extremely difficult to identify the quality. The main condition is that the fiber is uniform and the color is bright and clean as the superior grade. Some cotton merchants often mix bone powder, lead powder, etc. into the cotton in order to increase the weight and whiten the color. This kind of silk floss has a very good appearance, but the internal quality is very bad, and even after one or two years, it cannot be re-lined. Customers must pay attention: As for the silk floss mixed with kapok, the internal quality is even worse!

In short, silk floss is undeniably a good tool for winter warmth. In the current promotion of national products, I think it is worth introducing to readers.

One Person Cannot Carry It Alone 239

Interview Record

A Record of Market Inspection in Southeast Asia (1) 240

— Ji Ping

–A Conversation with Mr. Xiang Kangyuan–

The prerequisite for developing the national products industry is of course to expand the market as the first condition. Many people advocate developing in the country, but in recent years, rural areas in the interior have gone bankrupt, and people's livelihoods have been deteriorating, making it difficult to promote national products. Therefore, some people advocate developing in the Southeast Asian islands, because there are more than 10 million overseas Chinese in Southeast Asia, who are all patriotic and like to use national products, but national products are not easy to buy and there is simply nowhere to buy them. If we take this opportunity to promote sales in that area as much as possible, it is indeed very promising. However, the promotion method is by no means effective if manufacturers proceed alone. We must unite our efforts and have a group organization before we can proceed. On this point, Mr. Xiang Kangyuan first advocated, believing that this is the most effective method. Mr. Xiang's advocacy is not based on empty talk. He has personally inspected the Southeast Asian market, and what he has seen and heard is more accurate. I will publish his opinions publicly for the reference of those who are enthusiastic about the national products industry. (Note: This article was originally written for the "Southeast Asia Intelligence" of Jinan University) Development of Southeast Asian Trade Special Issue)

(Question) Can you tell us about your motive for traveling to Southeast Asia this time?

(Answer) I know the close relationship between the Southeast Asian islands and our country. A long time ago, I wanted to travel there in person and enjoy the scenery of the South. However, due to the constraints of my duties, I have not been able to do so for a long time. This time, in order to understand the commercial situation in Southeast Asia and report the factory affairs to Mr. Hu Wenhu, the chairman of our factory (namely Kangyuan Printing and Can Making Factory), I decided to set off.

(Question) How has the trade of overseas Chinese in Southeast Asia changed?

(Answer) According to my personal observation, the changes in the trade of overseas Chinese in Southeast Asia can be divided into five periods:

(1) Chinese merchants sell goods from Fujian and Guangdong and trade with the local people

(2) Chinese merchants sell goods from Fujian and Guangdong and trade with the local people

(3) Chinese merchants sell British goods and trade with the local people

(4) Chinese merchants boycott Japanese goods, and Japanese merchants trade directly with the local people;

(5) The colonial government implements restrictions on the import of Japanese goods in order to protect its domestic industry and commerce.

Because the Southeast Asian islands are the land opened up by our compatriots, the power of overseas Chinese has always been very great. Although the political power was later seized by Westerners, the economic power has always been in the hands of the overseas Chinese. About fifty years ago, almost all of the daily necessities of the local people were exported from Fujian and Guangdong. The overseas Chinese are all from Fujian and Guangdong. Based on the concept of loving their hometowns, they tried their best to promote the products of their hometowns to the local people in Southeast Asia. The local people felt that the goods from Fujian and Guangdong were novel and useful, so they were naturally happy to purchase them. During this period, Chinese merchants engaged in light-profit and heavy-trade transactions, so there were many who started their fortunes by this. Over a period of time, the machine industry in various European countries flourished, and our country's natural products and handicrafts were all defeated by them, thus occupying the original position of Chinese merchants. This is not surprising, Darwin's theory of evolution does not say "survival of the fittest"? Our products are not as beautiful as theirs, so you are not allowed to stand. Chinese merchants were hit by this and had to "catch up" to sell Western goods, especially British goods, to earn meager profits to maintain their lives. Changing from self-operating merchants to intermediary merchants planted the root of Western economic aggression. In the past ten years, Japan's industry has suddenly revitalized, and the whole country has been chanting the so-called "Southward Policy," and first used economic aggression as a pioneer to desperately dump industrial products to Southeast Asia. They have the power of politics as their backing, the transportation industry is developed, and the cost is relatively low. The same goods are cheaper than Western goods, and naturally welcomed by the local people, so the position of the Southeast Asian market has been dominated by Japanese goods. At that time, our overseas Chinese merchants had to go along with the trend and engage in the sale of Japanese goods. Before long, the Sino-Japanese issue gradually became tense. After the September 18th Incident, the situation was dangerous, and diplomatic relations broke down. Driven by conscience, our overseas Chinese aroused nationalistic thoughts and implemented an economic boycott of patriotic movement. All Japanese goods were refused to be sold. The Japanese are really good at observing the situation and changing their views. Since the Chinese merchants did not cooperate, they tried to trade directly with the local people. Japanese merchants are rich in experience in market promotion, coupled with the words "cheap and good quality" to attract the attention of the local people, it is naturally easy to get started. In addition to opening self-operated stores in various ports in Southeast Asia, Japanese merchants even have stores in the inland villages and towns. The facades are beautifully decorated, and radio tape recorders sing all day long, almost attracting the souls of the local people. The prosperity of the business can be imagined. There are also many shameless Western stores that are also promoting Japanese goods. If it were not for the colonial government's increase in tariff barriers, Japanese goods would simply be like mercury leaking to the ground and there would be no holes to enter. (To be continued)

Free Talk

"Seeing off at the Wattle Gate, the Moonlight is Fresh" 241

— Jiang Jiping

In Kuta Hakuson's "Views on Nature Poetry of the East and West," there is a very interesting point recorded. He said, "Like that Erasmus, who was proficient in ancient literature and had a great deal of education, when someone asked him what he saw when he passed through the Alps, what touched his heart, he replied: 'Only the stench of a gloomy inn, and wine that was sour enough to kill a man.' This is indeed written in his letters. Going from Switzerland to Italy, the beauty of the mountains covered with snow for ten thousand years did not move his heart at all." This kind of person is simply too insensitive. The high monks of the European Middle Ages, when they traveled in Switzerland, are said to have stubbornly turned their heads away and refused to look at the beauty of the mountains and rivers, and this kind of person is a bit pretentious. In fact, literature and art are things that follow the times. What kind of literature and art we need in this era, we should have what kind of works produced. For example, taking the issue of rural areas, the ancient countryside is different from the modern countryside. Now there are still people who yearn to be pastoral poets, like Tao Yuanming, "Spring and autumn have many good days, climbing high and composing new poems. Passing the door and calling to each other, with wine to drink and measure. Farm work is done separately, and leisure often brings mutual longing. When longing arises, we put on our clothes, and talking and laughing never tire." I believe that modern farmers do not necessarily have that kind of joy. The countryside in the time of Du Fu and Wang Wei was "White sand, green bamboo, a river village at dusk; seeing off at the wattle gate, the moonlight is fresh." It was "The setting sun shines on the village, cattle and sheep return to the poor lane. The old man thinks of the shepherd boy, leaning on his staff, waiting at the wattle door." This is the situation of the ancient countryside, and I believe that the modern countryside certainly does not have such beautiful scenery, and the farmers certainly do not have that kind of leisurely mood of "seeing off at the wattle gate, the moonlight is fresh." The farmers' cattle and sheep may have been stewed by bandits and warlords, and the wattle door may have been demolished and burned. The old man may be locked in a prison sighing, and the shepherd boy may have already run to the city to pull a rickshaw. The various elements that constitute the beauty of the countryside have now changed. What it looks like when it's all broken apart, we who were not born in the countryside, of course, don't know very well, but if we close our eyes and think about it, the modern Chinese countryside is not very good-looking. I don't quite believe that there is still a village living a happy life, with a very fat and beautiful rooster crowing on the firewood, and a very pretty and simple little girl smiling shyly at strangers. There are beautiful peach blossoms in the yard, and you can go in and pick a branch to play with. If you are thirsty, you can go into the house and drink a bowl of water. If you happen to be there during mealtime, the host will let you eat something, and say, "The old man's family is poor, only old wine is available." I'm afraid this era has long passed. I know that modern, better villages have several guns. If a stranger goes there, they will probably think you are a scout for kidnappers. At night, the sound of gunfire is crackling and popping everywhere. If a pastoral poet from the city happens to live in the countryside for a day and a half, he will surely think that it is the sound of firecrackers on New Year's Eve. In the eyes of pastoral poets, everything is beautiful. The burnt, crooked houses, the plow for plowing the fields lying diagonally on the edge of the field, the green grass more than the rice, the trees with their tops cut off, and the well without anyone drawing water, with a board placed on it, these things, in the eyes of pastoral poets drinking coffee and tea, may be considered an unexpected beautiful scene. They are just like the high monks of the European Middle Ages, stubbornly turning their heads away and refusing to look at such a desolate scene in the countryside. Some time ago, I saw a piece of news saying that a certain place in the Northeast was recruiting workers to work, with a daily wage of two yuan and especially good treatment. So farmers from a certain place sold their family property to pay for travel expenses, and supported the old and carried the young to go to work. Until they reached a certain place, they met a group of previously recruited workers who said that the place not only did not give two yuan in wages, but was also extremely abusive. Everyone heard this and cried, hugging each other, because their way of life had been cut off, and they could not go back. The road ahead was茫茫, and they really didn't know what to do. Everyone thought that there was no other way but to cry, or else to die! I heard that someone is trying to provide relief, and I think it will just be giving everyone two corn buns to eat and be done with it. But the news of giving corn buns has not been heard to this day, and it may just fade away like this, and we don't know! From this small group of farmers, we can speculate on the situation of the modern Chinese countryside. Yet our poets, our artists, are still writing "Seeing off at the wattle gate, the moonlight is fresh!"

December 22nd, in Tianjin

Christmas Concert 242

— Bai She

By chance, I entered the Moore Church, where a beautiful Christmas tree was erected in front of the door, and joined the black-robed pastors and the men and women of the choir, the white-collared gentlemen and the conductor of the string orchestra, the pure yellow-faced sacred virgins, the Christians wearing metal crosses, the large BASS, and all kinds of people "coming together to offer congratulations and toast." I'm not lying, this is the first time in my life that I've done this.

I usually don't have much spare money to buy tickets for concerts, but I have a great love for music, especially the kind of formal, religious music, which I have experienced very little. Therefore, this time I entered the "holy land," it can be said that I was driven by a kind of curiosity.

After the grand and solemn ceremony was held in the inner hall, someone handed me a brochure for the Christmas concert. It was exquisitely printed on high-quality Chinese paper. I looked at it and knew that today's performance would be Messiah. It was the first public performance in China. It was composed by George Frideric Handel, with lyrics entirely from the scriptures, selected by Charles Jennens. It was divided into three parts: the first part was Prophecy and Fulfillment, the second part was Passion and Triumph, and the third part was Resurrection and Glory. At the beginning, there was also a solemn, harmonious, and joyful overture, interspersed with the ancient song "Pastoral Music" passed down in the rural areas of Calabria, Italy. The entire piece was divided into fifty-three sections, and it would take a full four hours to sing it completely.

I really didn't expect what kind of effect a religious latent force would have on people's hearts? But after listening to the choir's singing, I seemed to have found the answer. When the tenor soloist sang the amazing chant, SAIHYORU GODSPEAK YECOMPORTBLYTOLCROSALENI, the entire audience was immediately silent, without a trace of sound. The hall was filled with wisdom, ability, dignity, glory, and praise. It was impossible for me not to believe that there was such a thing as God in this world. I was really surprised, and it can be said that my entire spirit was captivated by this harmonious and solemn tone. I didn't know that I existed. I only knew that this was an environment full of ancient style, wisdom, dignity, and glory. This was the kingdom of Christ, the kingdom of the King of Kings.

The concert was performed section by section in order. A low chant from the contralto seemed to me to be listening to the whispers of the gods. Then, the mysterious sacred light was dazzling on the high cross. Adam, Eve, this is a very beautiful and abundant orchard······.

The strings suddenly slowed down, and finally died out. Then the hall erupted in a clamor, and the music conference was over.

Walking out of this holy land, this kingdom, the sky was drizzling with light rain. We, these people who "came together to offer congratulations and toast," suddenly became a flock of sheep in the dark night, but there was no glory of the Lord shining around. Standing in the rain waiting for the car, I suddenly realized like lightning: Messiah, sacred song, you spirit of music! Your "name must be called wonderful" because you are omnipotent.

Returning from the Volcano (6) 243

— Lan Ru

The magnificent volcano

Has finally been reached!

Wisp after wisp of green smoke spews out from the mouth of the abyss, and my spirit suddenly becomes excited, and my steps are especially fast. My body is as light as a bird, and I am the first to walk to the crater teahouse.

This is a tea pavilion made of wooden planks. It can hold more than thirty people, and there is tea to drink, as well as fruit and soda water for sale, but there is no food to eat. At this time, the people resting inside and outside the crater teahouse are all watching me with tired smiles, and some old women are carefully looking at me from the top of my head to my heels.

There are two classmates standing at the crater teahouse who came with us all the way, and I almost don't recognize them. It turns out that everyone's face is covered with a layer of black ash mask.

The crater teahouse is the highest hill on the volcano, and the volcanic vent is still below. This section of the road is even more difficult to walk, because walking on sharp, multi-angled lava, you will break your skin if you fall down carelessly. At this time, I understood the blurred faces with bloodstains that I saw in the desert just now. It turned out that they were injured here. Although my heart was thinking that I should look at the ground and walk carefully, my eyes were actually staring far away at the gray-black smoke that was suddenly冒出来 from the crater in a daze.

The crater is here!

My spirit suddenly tensed up! The surrounding scenery immediately became solemn, magnificent, gloomy, and miserable. Everyone standing next to the volcano and looking down said in a terrifying and trembling tone: "Danger! The crater is really deep!"

No one had a smile on their face, and their eyes were all focused on the dark crater of the abyss. Maybe some of their friends had committed suicide here, and their sadness and sentimentality were beyond our imagination.

Before I came to the volcano, Jian'er told me: "The volcano cannot be visited. I don't know why, it has a kind of magic that lures every young man and woman. Everyone who has been there once always lingers on the volcano, and when they go there a second time, they bury their lives there."

At first, I absolutely didn't believe this, but once I got there, I was indeed bewitched by the magnificent volcano. I forgot the mission I was carrying, forgot the world, forgot all my relatives and friends. I wanted to die a tragic death, jump down, and end this painful and difficult life: but Dante's shadow immediately stood in front of me, his solemn face stopped me. His powerful arms embraced me, causing me to shiver unconsciously and take a step back.

"Dangerous!" A policeman guarding the mouth of the volcano said to me: he gestured to drive me away.

"Minasha, don't say SAYOUNARA to us!"

Ms. Yang was still joking with me, even though she was panting.

About Poetry 244

— Jun Han

As an editor of a literary journal, one must have this experience: among the manuscripts he receives, poetry probably accounts for the majority, but there are few mature works! Or, if you happily go to a middle school to visit, as long as you carefully browse the journals and wall newspapers run by the students, most of the materials on them are also poetry, even so much that it surprises you.

Why is there so much poetry in particular? Maybe it's because poetry is easy to write? Isn't it?

Now, since we are talking about poetry, you must understand that first of all, you must recognize the particularity of the language used in poetry and the ideas suitable for poetry. Because thought and language are closely and inseparably combined, the technique of writing poetry is to use words to fix emotional experiences. Therefore, poetry has emotional, vivid, and metaphorical main components. Since words are used to fix emotional experiences, then poetry is the medium of emotion. However, these emotions and experiences are historical, social, and human emotions and experiences. Therefore, poetry does not belong to the poet personally, but is a product of society. It is a kind of abstract, historical, and social function. At the same time, it reflects the characteristics of the times in its own form. Broadly speaking, the subjective and objective significance of the social function of poetry is the reproduction of experience and personality education, and the reproduction of mass psychology.

If poets knew that poetry is a product of society, I'm afraid they would no longer be willing to groan without illness and produce shoddy works, right?

Finally, Mr. Editors of literary journals, don't neglect the large number of poems submitted. You must carefully select and discard them. The large number of poems is the reason for production. Perhaps it is not because poetry is easy to write, but because poetry at the current stage is relatively easy to express the emotions of the current society, right?

Mother and Son 245

— Yi An

Cocoon (6) 246

— Original by Lin Fusao, translated by Shizuko

About a week later, he sent a letter.

(This morning, after picking up my mother's bones, they were completely packed into a jar that was less than seven inches high. Placing this jar in front of me, I deeply felt that this was a huge blow.

"When the funeral was held, ten female workers from the factory came. Those were probably all loved by my mother. It is said that there were even more people who were also requesting the factory to let them come to the funeral at least once, but of course the factory did not agree. And they all knew that they would be punished for running away. 丨This really makes my chest feel blocked and depressed.

"During the New Year's holiday, when my mother forbade me to drop out of school, I had made a plan. I wanted to find something to do with my own hands after entering university. In this way, I would also have a scholarship, so that my mother would no longer have to work, and my mother and son would undoubtedly be able to live. This plan lifted my spirits and gave me the courage to go back to school! However, now, what else can I say!

"With the urn in front of me, I thought丨丨about the invisible force that silently sucked away my mother's life, the organization of the world."

"Gradually shrinking two, gradually enlarged silk thread丨丨" Ink-black corpse of a pupa!

"My mother looked forward to my coming out of the mountains, this was her only hope. I also paid attention to fulfilling that hope. I only worked hard for this purpose丨However, what about now!

"But I don't despair. When I was picking up my mother's bones by candlelight in the crematorium in the mountains, a thought suddenly came to my mind. I felt that a new path had been opened up. 丨Cocoons are not just one! Suffering is not just for my mother!

"Even in this country we live in, millions, no," tens of millions of people, are like cocoons in boiling water, with an invisible blood vessel behind their backs, constantly sucking their lives.

"You may think it strange that I suddenly said such a thing, but I know who the opponent in the battle is. I will always have time to talk about the details. I suddenly remembered the time in middle school when I drew my knife to confront those who bullied me. But the path I am going to take in the future is not such a despicable path. It is a job that a man can bet his life on. My mother would also like it.

"I won't be coming back to school anymore, and I won't be able to meet you for a while. Please study hard and take care of yourself.

"Also, in the left drawer of my desk, there is a white cocoon. It is a wonderful souvenir, a souvenir of my mother. I would like to respectfully present it to you."

It has been ten years since then.

Even now, whenever I see a cocoon, I can't help but think of Sakai Yasuo. However, as I said before, I am a city dweller who can only see the moon and reeds in the display window to feel that autumn has arrived, and I hardly have the opportunity to see a cocoon.

But now, because I want to remember him, I don't particularly need to see a cocoon. (The End)

Yesterday and the day before, due to the Christmas holiday, the gold and foreign exchange markets were closed. The customs gold unit decreased by 0.001, and the gold standard price retreated to 1012 yuan and 9 jiao, because the overseas silver market rose only slightly, the exchange rate was average, and the price of raw gold in London fell by half a penny. The British exchange rate increased by 0.0625, calculated at one shilling, five pence, and three-one-two-five. As for the foreign exchange and gold markets, they will be closed as usual today.

The American Yellow Eagle Brand Black Iron Sheet is in Great Demand and There are Rumors of Hoarding 261

The American Yellow Eagle brand black iron sheet is an essential product for enamel factories, so each enamel factory must purchase this type of variety from the United States. Because of its superior material and soft nature, its selling price exceeds that of ordinary goods on the market, estimated at 12 to 13 yuan per dan. In the industry, only a few firms specializing in enamel factories and enamel factories purchase it. The remaining firms do not purchase it, so there are very few of these goods circulating on the market. Now that the enamel business is not very developed, the amount of goods purchased by each factory is also less than in previous years. Recently, each factory has suddenly experienced a shortage panic, so they are searching for it on the market. However, the inventory is extremely low, so those holding the goods have the intention of monopolizing and hoarding. As a result, the market price has risen sharply and has not stopped. The estimated price is 14 yuan, and it is heard that factories are still purchasing a small amount.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Fifteen Yuan Per Person for a Big Meal 284

— Blowing

The day before yesterday was Christmas Day. All countries in the world celebrated the birthday of Jesus. The national palace hosted a banquet for 700 poor people. The German capital entertained 12,000 poor children. Austria granted amnesty to show Jesus's spirit of sacrificing himself to save people. Shanghai, because it has so many Western residents, therefore welcomed the night of revelry. A certain garden dance floor and restaurant's business was very prosperous for five yuan, and announced that it was full. The dance floor was also extremely crowded. Green wine and red lights, what kind of world is this?

Fifteen yuan per person for a big meal is originally not surprising. Some restaurants sell each big meal for thirty or forty foreign yuan. Some restaurants sell each big meal for up to fifty or sixty foreign yuan. This kind of big meal is only for important people from various countries and wealthy merchants to learn from. Poor scholars cannot even talk about trying it. It is said that on the day before yesterday, in a certain garden, only one-tenth of the foreign gentlemen came to learn from it, and our compatriots who came to learn from it were as many as nine-tenths. Such a place of entertainment, a night of revelry, life in this world, grand events are not always held. "Enjoy today's wine today, worry about tomorrow when there's no money tomorrow." This is originally what several gentlemen with minds as bright as "fireflies" do.

There's a saying: "A rich family's banquet, a poor man's half-year's food." This ancient saying should still be revised now. "A rich man's meal, a poor man's year's food." This year, famine is everywhere, and the number of disaster victims is too difficult to count. Tree bark and grass roots cannot even provide a full meal, and people are even starving to death in ditches everywhere. According to yesterday's newspaper report, the relief association sent a large number of people to various provinces for disaster relief. A total of nineteen provinces suffered from disasters. Starting today, they will first go to Anhui, Jiangxi, and other six provinces to investigate and provide relief. The relief funds require 30 million yuan, etc. Because there are so many disaster victims, 30 million yuan has been raised. How much can each hungry person get? If the gentlemen attending that night could save one big meal, it would be saving the lives of several hungry people. If you add the cost of dancing, it would be enough to save the lives of dozens or even hundreds of people. It's truly "behind the vermilion gates, meat and wine are left to rot; on the road lie the bones of those frozen to death." Isn't this kind of phenomenon enough to move your sinking minds?

"Embracing a bosom full of soft jade and fragrant warmth, ah! Liu Ruan entered Tiantai!" Who can break this kind of confusing front? They would rather sacrifice their lives and ruin their families to save enchanting and beautiful dancers than save a meal and a dance to save hungry people dying in ditches. Therefore, some people say that humans are emotional animals. Looking at it from this perspective, I don't believe that this statement has any truth. Xunzi said, "Human nature is evil; those who do good are false." His words are somewhat similar. Therefore, "At the beginning of man, his nature is good," this kind of book is originally deceptive and should be burned.

The Spring of Zishi Street 285

— New Green

The third year of Xining in the Song Dynasty's Shenzong era.

It was a beautiful spring that couldn't be dispelled.

Pan Jinlian walked Wang Po to the door. Returning to her bedroom, she felt an inexplicable heat in her body, and sweat oozed from her back like rice paste.

Pushing open the ancient louvered phoenix-tail window, there was no wind outside. Willow catkins floated, floated, like cotton.

"Ah! It's already the season of falling flowers, no wonder the weather is so hot."

She leaned lazily against the window, picking her teeth with a small bamboo stick, looking at the white clouds in the sky, planning how to enjoy a joyful tomorrow. Those handsome eyes, that prominent nose, that tall and strange face, that clear and charming voice, ah! My Ximen Qing, my beloved Ximen Qing: You are truly the source of my life, the treasure of my soul.

She smiled. She rejoiced that she had achieved victory and was able to hide it from Wu Dalang, who was nominally her husband but actually as withered as a child, and satisfyingly obtain a new lover. | | Ximen Qing | |

She planned, how to send Wu Dalang out tomorrow? And what kind of words to use to tell him to spend the night in Yuncheng? When he | | Ximen Qing | | comes, what generous and kind way should I use to greet him? How should I entertain him? And how should I express my full enthusiasm to him? How should I tell him about my myriad thoughts? She decided: first, embrace him and give him a hearty kiss to vent the five years of suffering 丨 丨 丨 not married to 丨 丨 not sold to 丨 丨 Wu Dalang for five full years.

Thinking of the happy times, the blood boiled throughout her body, and her limbs and bones felt as comfortable and light as if they had been ironed with an iron.

Suddenly, another dark shadow, like a sharp arrow, painfully gnawed at her heart. "Honor," "A woman's most precious honor!" She understood that once she fell in love with Ximen Qing, not only would she be subject to the most severe moral sanctions and be despised by everyone, but perhaps the discovery of the crime would also lead to unimaginable punishments. And that cruel punishment would inevitably be a severe sentence ending her life's journey. She hysterically fantasized about the final, inevitable stage: it seemed that a layer of black mist was covering her eyes, and in the mist, she was already tied to a small cart, with a burly man escorting her in a parade on the street. As she walked, she shouted, and countless men and women, old and young, pointed at her and cursed:

"Look at the shameless slut!"

"Look at the slut who poisoned her husband and deserves to die!"

Ah! Slut, such a terrible slut. She suddenly shuddered, and cold sweat soaked through her skin. As if waking from a dream, she pinched her leg hard and fiercely. She gently called out to herself:

"Pan Jinlian! Pan Jinlian! You've been smart your whole life, don't be confused for a moment and do something despicable to shame your ancestors!"

She quickly bit off the small bamboo stick she used to pick her teeth, expressing her determination to jump out of the trap. She realized that this was a critical moment of distinguishing between good and evil, humans and beasts. She wanted to move upwards, she wanted to be human, and she had to tearfully abandon her and Ximen Qing's first love affair. She casually opened the calendar hanging on the rosewood bamboo bed and silently recited the "Jade Calendar Response Chapter" attached to the end of the scroll, trying to use the power of the imperial Taoist gods to dissipate the emotions that were about to erupt. But in fact, although she tried her best to restrain herself from thinking about Ximen Qing again, Ximen Qing's shadow lingered around her, making it impossible for her to escape. In an instant, a thousand troops and ten thousand horses were galloping in her mind:

Handsome eyes... prominent nose... his tall and strange face... clear and charming voice... slut! slut!

Her fluctuating nerves were as chaotic as a tangled pile of firewood. She felt a terrible suffocation and painfully clenched her teeth. Her face was as red as fire.

There was no sound in the courtyard, under the clear sky.

In the spring breeze, a song faintly drifted over:

"Drink! This mead-like mellow wine,

Rejoice! This flower-like spring night;

Youth will not return, time easily grows old!

Wait for the years to change,

Winning only white hair."

She listened blankly to the song and then sobbed softly.

When the Sun Slants 286

— Ding Weinan

The smoke from the cooking fires billows out of the thicket over there, at this time when the sun slants: somewhat softly embracing these forests, not letting people see, the light red that it smears, some of it quietly seeps into the clouds, slowly assimilating into the haziness of the cloud shadows, in the fleeting moment of the setting sun's afterglow, and it is vividly transforming in the midst of nature!

The red halo of twilight covers the face of the western sky, like the face of a banqueter who has drunk mellow wine to the point of intoxication; this great intoxicated-like vast sky is nurturing boundless commotion. The clouds are so drifting, but sometimes they will gradually transform in this azure sky, but when she approaches this western sky at dusk, she will put on rouge on her face just like the modern girls in today's city. Of course, this kind of dressing up is also to charm the vast sky, right?

On the wilderness under the cloud shadows and the sky's overlook, and on the protruding mountain peaks, small shadows of people and animals are scattered, with many quivering white dots, naturally these are flocks of sheep. There are sounds of laughter and the singing of pastoral songs, this here is naturally a few herding children. The people in the fields over there, of course, are farmers, diligently doing the growth of what they hope for, afraid that the sun will fall down immediately, they are hurrying to do what they inevitably need to do. Autumn harvest is now already

Page 18

not good, not doing other things, preparing for the spring planting work, would be even worse. In their hearts, there is only working hard, moreover the current "famine" is firmly stuck to their bodies. Their burdens include their children who are crying out for food, the weakness of their aging parents, the unbearable cold, and the burden of taxes, ah, these oppressions are unavoidable and will come upon them from time to time, loosening their grip even for a moment will lead to starvation: but there will be even more terrible things to come, that is, inexplicable man-made disasters and tragic natural disasters! Now they are working diligently, afraid that there will be nothing to do tomorrow, and furthermore, that cursed sun, ah, it is tired and wants to hide below the horizon to rest. Those crows are even more deceitful, cawing and calling their companions, "It's night, it's night," preparing to return to their nests to sleep. The flocks of geese are also flying in lines towards the sky, and what is fanned up under their wings is bringing the milky white news of the night.

The women at home are busy cooking dinner. The clothes and children's diapers that were drying on the racks outside are all gone. The sparrows on the eaves are chirping and preparing to go into the crevices of the tiles, afraid that their companions have not yet returned, as if they are calling out there. In the hall, the chickens are clucking and walking to their roosts on their own, the dim room is even dimmer, the fire in the stove in the kitchen is red, and the pot is cooking dishes, preparing for the weary husband or her son to return.

The children in the wilderness are driving the cattle and sheep, whistling and going home vaguely, closing the cattle well, tethering the sheep well, and running towards the kitchen, clamoring to their mother and older sister for food. With their innocent hearts, they do not understand the struggles of their parents!

At this time, the curtain of night is high, and they are still working hard: the wilderness is hazy, and the distant forests and mountains are naturally combined into a pitch-black mass. The sounds of birds are not heard, only the violent sounds of owls are howling in the black forest, beginning its cruel behavior. Dimly, there is only the floating of the night, the pulse of the night, filling their pain, their sorrow, their hard work!

The Concubines Raise Their Heads 287

— Yang An

A dispatch from Nanjing was published in various newspapers the other day, which read:

"The Judicial Yuan, based on a telegram from the Qinghai Higher Court requesting an interpretation of whether a 'head of household' has the right to file charges in cases of a concubine committing adultery, has been resolved by the Yuan's Uniform Interpretation of Laws Conference. Since the 'head of household' and the concubine do not have a spousal relationship, the 'head of household' naturally has no right to file charges when the concubine commits adultery with another. This decision has been telegraphed back for notification."

This is a rather pleasing matter. In China, the popularity of taking concubines truly surpasses all other nations. Anyone with a bit of property generally seeks happiness in this area. Having one concubine is not enough, and after a while, they become tiresome, so they acquire another, and another, and another, until there are countless. For example, the late Zhang Zongchang did not even know how many concubines he had. When he breathed his last, there were a considerable twenty-four who came forward to mourn. As for those who took only one or two concubines, they were too numerous to count within the four seas. The former Doctor of Law, Wang Chonghui, stated that he could not clearly define the crime of "a married man committing adultery" because three out of ten Chinese men took concubines. If they were to be convicted and sentenced to imprisonment, the whole country would be filled with prisons, so it was not possible to clearly define it as a crime. I think Dr. Wang's statistic is probably seventy to eighty percent accurate (whether his argument is correct or not is another question, and need not be discussed here). This shows how numerous concubines are in China.

Now, the judicial authorities have clearly stipulated that if a concubine commits adultery, the man has no right to file charges. This is truly a delightful event. I think that not only will the concubines rejoice, but those of us who see this will also applaud and cheer endlessly. (Please forgive me; I do not harbor any ill intentions.) Going forward, concubines, who have been deeply oppressed for thousands of years, although they may not be able to immediately reclaim their personal dignity, freedom, and independence, can at least engage in some scandalous behavior. For example, a petite and charming concubine of eighteen paired with a white-haired old man will definitely not be able to achieve balance in terms of sex alone, let alone satisfaction. This will very likely lead to extramarital affairs. If they are bold enough, they might as well do it openly, since the old man can catch them in the act but has no way to prosecute, leaving him to "beat the rocks and cry to heaven."

Men who love to take concubines, have you seen the telegram above? While women are certainly good for seeking pleasure, this time you have run into a major obstacle.

Amateur Mailbox

Treatment for Nocturnal Emission 288

Editor: I have long admired you as a guiding light for those who are lost and a mentor for the unfortunate. I have a problem that I would like you to answer. I am currently eighteen years old. I met a girlfriend last year who is kind and approachable, and I love her very much. Our feelings for each other are excellent. Recently, she suddenly proposed marriage, demanding that I marry her, but I dare not agree because I have an unspeakable difficulty. The thing is, when I was sixteen years old, I was young and ignorant, and impulsively masturbated, causing me to suffer from nocturnal emission for two years. Now, I have an emission about once every ten days, and I often experience dizziness and fatigue. I know the condition is not mild and want to see a doctor for treatment, but I don't know which doctor is the most suitable. If I don't seek treatment, will it interfere with marriage in terms of physiology? Because she and I are best friends, if it interferes, wouldn't I be harming her if we marry? The above question has made me hesitate for a long time. Due to concerns about my reputation, I dare not express it to others. I specifically ask for your reply. Also, I think there must be many pitiful people in the world who suffer from the same disease as me. If you would kindly publish your reply, the beneficiaries would be in the thousands, and not just me, who would be grateful beyond words. Yours respectfully, Jin Pinyi

Editor's Note: Many young people, due to external temptations and impulsive desires, commit masturbation, causing this kind of harmful error to their bodies. They feel pain in both body and mind and are filled with regret. However, we believe that nocturnal emission is not an incurable disease. As long as everyone can realize this, can be determined to change and start anew, then there is hope to eliminate this bad habit.

Regarding nocturnal emission, according to what the editor knows, there are two types: one is physiological, and the other is pathological. Physiological nocturnal emission is a phenomenon where a healthy body with strong blood and sufficient essence inevitably overflows, with one or two emissions per month. After the emission, there are no morbid states such as lack of energy. This type of nocturnal emission does not require treatment and will naturally stop after marriage. There is also a pathological nocturnal emission, which requires attention. Pathological nocturnal emission is mostly caused by masturbation, or evil thoughts during the day, or reading inappropriate books and paintings, etc. The milder symptoms are once every few days, and the severe ones are like this every day. The most severe becomes spermatorrhea, with emissions without dreams, and occasional hallucinations during the day, which immediately lead to emissions. After the emission, there is dizziness, blurred vision, fatigue, and the body gradually becomes emaciated. Some may even become infertile as a result. If not treated quickly, it is extremely dangerous. However, according to what general physicians say, drugs are rarely effective for nocturnal emission. It is necessary to resolutely eradicate past evil thoughts and habits, absolutely not to look at inappropriate books and paintings, not to watch certain tempting movies and dramas. At the same time, during the day, one should use proper work to exhaust one's body as much as possible so that one can sleep soundly at night. Alternatively, one can decide to study some science and concentrate all thoughts on this science, without thinking about anything else. If a person suffering from spermatorrhea can implement such fundamental treatment from all aspects, then his symptoms will definitely gradually heal.

Mr. Jin's nocturnal emission is pathological, but it does not seem to be severe, so he need not worry too much. As long as he can be determined to implement the above methods, I think he will certainly regain his health and enjoy the pleasures of life. However, it is best not to talk about marriage for the time being until the emissions stop. If the other party misunderstands, you can get engaged first and then set a date for the wedding in a year or two. Furthermore, Mr. Jin is only eighteen years old now, and there seems to be no need to rush into marriage.

Opening Piece "End of the Year"

Busy and rushed until the end of the year. Winter with wind and snow in the twelfth month. Wealthy families have everything prepared. They have already prepared wine and sacrifices to the ancestors. The whole family gathers for a feast and drinks wine. Collecting rent and settling accounts, gold and silver are abundant. Acquiring property and adding more fields. There is still surplus capital to generate interest. Poor people suffer the most at the end of the year. Their hearts are filled with worry like oil being fried. Last time, they paid official grain and private debts. Clothing, firewood, rice, and other necessities are not enough. Children cry, daughters wail, and female servants complain. They beg relatives and friends, revealing their shame. Begging and pleading are useless. They only provoke separation and cold laughter. Rushing and scurrying until the thirtieth of the year. The sound of the drum echoes, and they sigh in despair. The ancients said that the poor look forward to the coming year. How can one dig a well when one is already thirsty? Remember to prepare ahead of time.

Ten years a dream of Yangzhou,

Shenbao Local Supplement Movie Special

Good Intentions Become Bad Intentions: Movie Stars' Greatest Fear is Fans 295

— Li Bin

There's a Western saying that snails are animals undisturbed by the outside world, only able to hear extremely loud noises. However, movie stars, whether Chinese or foreign, especially those in Hollywood, cannot enjoy such tranquility. Because of their status, they are often subjected to special disturbances from the outside world. Even the adoration of fans, although stemming from admiration, sometimes increases their suffering. Thus, good intentions turn into bad ones. As for the curiosity of fans, treating stars like monkeys in a cage, that makes stars feel even more embarrassed.

Marlene Dietrich originally lived a leisurely and happy life in Hollywood. Later, a newspaper published her photo with her home address noted underneath. As a result, the number of people making pilgrimages to her house every day was countless, some walking, some driving, some cycling. They constantly rang her doorbell, sat on her lawn, and parked their cars haphazardly in front of her gate. One day, things got out of hand. An entire family arrived, bringing three generations of ancestors with them. They treated Marlene's lawn as their campsite. They brought cameras, autograph books, telescopes, and picnic food. At noon, they gathered for a meal, opening cans of salted olives, tins of sardines, and jars of pickled cucumbers. The bottles, cans, paper wrappers, eggshells, sweet potato peels, etc., were scattered all over the ground. The younger ones jumped and shouted. The middle-aged ones pretended to pick flowers, peering into the windows. The elderly slept in the sun, smoking and reading newspapers. They were all waiting for the star to come out and greet them. They waited until late at night, and when she didn't appear, they left. A week later, Marlene Dietrich moved.

Everyone says that camera work is a necessary path to fame for movie stars. However, stars fear cameras outside the studio most, especially beautiful male and female stars. Because in the studio, the cameraman must make them look good, with appropriate angles, and prevent their shortcomings from being exposed. But once outside the studio, they have no protection whatsoever. Unprepared photos have become a temporary trend. The group of people who steal photos of stars must wait for the stars to be inattentive, or extremely funny and ugly, or in embarrassing situations, so the photos can be sensational and win. Therefore, a dollar spent on a simple camera can produce results as bad as those taken by an expert. The expert, on the other hand, has to go to great lengths to capture unexpected photos of stars. Only these grotesque photos can be sold for money. But these grotesque photos are what stars hate most. However, they cannot avoid the attacks of malicious cameras.

Hunting for stars' autographs is as feared and unavoidable by stars as hunting for their photos. In unfortunate situations, a star can be surrounded by a hunting group, and signing their name for half an hour won't be enough to satisfy them. These signature hunters surround the entrance of the studio, guard the vicinity of the stars' residences, and patrol the hotels and places where stars often appear. Like photographers, they can be encountered on the streets, tennis courts, and boxing arenas. Recently, Joan Crawford encountered a group of people who stopped her car on the street, not letting her leave until she signed countless names, large and small. The largest was signed on the back of a coat. Watching movies is sometimes a necessary task for stars, but when they encounter curious people, they are at their wit's end. There is a kind of person called "pre-screening front row dogs". They rush into the theater early on the night of the first public screening and sit in the front row, right next to the seats specially reserved for the stars. When the lights go out, the movie starts, and the stars arrive, they turn around and kneel on their seats to watch the movie stars. It's not so bad if they just watch, but they block the stars' view.

The attacks of the crowd are also something that stars fear. They can encounter unexpected events before and after performing on stage, at the entrance of the theater, and in the studio. Compared to such attacks, signing a few names or giving people some funny photos seems much kinder. Maurice Chevalier was once surrounded by a group of middle-aged, plump ladies as soon as he stepped out of the dressing room. After introducing themselves, they suddenly launched a preemptive strike, everyone acting at once, some pulling his tie, some grabbing his handkerchief, some tearing the buttons off his clothes. Chevalier, seeing that the situation was not good, turned around and ran back. He fled into the dressing room and immediately closed the door. But he thought that these women, who could run into the studio, must have something to do with business. He couldn't afford to offend them, so he opened the window and waved to them with a smile, but he didn't dare go down again.

In the eyes of stars, journalists are respected but kept at a distance. They dare not offend them, nor dare they avoid them. Anyone who treats journalists arrogantly and rudely, offending them, they will unite and, without launching a blatant attack, simply resist a little passively, and then you are doomed. The recent failure of Katharine Hepburn's performance in New York can serve as an example. Tracing back to the beginning, the reason why journalists follow stars to collect news is nothing more than out of good intentions, admiration, and a willingness to do free publicity.

Movie Reviews

Review of "Rebirth Flower" - New Light 296

— Ling He

After "Sister Flowers" broke the box office record for Chinese films, it caused a great uproar, which led some film writers to pay attention to the reasons for the success of "Sister Flowers." Other works were also more or less influenced by "Sister Flowers," and it was no accident that the author of "Sister Flowers" came up with a sequel under this reputation.

In attracting a large audience to watch "Sister Flowers," when they had never been interested in Chinese films, the author of "Sister Flowers" certainly made a great contribution. At the same time, "Sister Flowers" is also an immortal record in the history of Chinese cinema. However, what worries us is that Chinese film writers are catering to the audience's tendency and cannot bravely correct it. That is to say, when the audience accepts the film, the writers cannot bravely further improve the audience's appreciation level. For example, everything in "Rebirth Flower" has not exceeded "Sister Flowers" in any way. It is in the same rut as "Sister Flowers."

"Sister Flowers" is the highest-grossing sound film in China. "Rebirth Flower" is also a sound film, but ordinary people do not feel very satisfied after watching these two works, when they have seen many advanced foreign sound films. Furthermore, the audience needs highly developed sound films. For example, the success of "Peach and Plum Calamity" has won a lot of praise from the audience, which proves that people are demanding that Chinese sound films strive to improve their standards.

There is no doubt that "Rebirth Flower" is the same as "Sister Flowers," whether in terms of content or creative techniques. Here, the author's consistent style is maintained, and like the latter part of "Daughter's Sutra," those so-called revolutionary sermons and the posture of those revolutionaries really make us unable to believe that it is a true depiction. If we observe from the costumes of the characters in the play, the so-called revolutionary ladies of Erbao's type, of course, refer to the present, which is explained in the most fashionable cheongsam. Then, in the author's view, the officials and warlords played by Da Xinyuan, Tan Zhiyuan, Wang Xianzai and others in the same era as Erbao should all have their "lives taken away". However, from the costumes of the Northern Warlords, we understand that it was the previous generation who were being revolutionised, and those unprincipled revolutionary heroes were also figures of the previous generation. ...... Here, the author's cleverness is fully expressed.

In addition, the relatively messy editing and the lack of sophistication in the dialogue have prevented the film from achieving full success. Other things are omitted.

Audience Feedback

Talking about "Bigamy" 297

— Yafei

I just came back from Suzhou and saw "Bigamy" being screened at New Light. I was dragged by a friend to watch it.

That's right, "Bigamy" is Wu Cun's first contribution after joining Star, and it is also the first collaboration between Gao Zhanfei and Gao Qianping. We have read Wang Pingling's article on the content of this story in the "Literary Monthly", but today, what we see on the screen is very different from what was in the article. Perhaps this is because articles and movies cannot be expressed in the same way?

Here, the playwright only grasped a very ordinary story, but because of the appropriate handling and the vivid personalities of the characters, it can easily arouse the audience's empathy.

It depicts an old couple in the countryside who are diligent and thrifty in their lives. When they send their son away to study, they recall their love and hard work twenty years ago. They eagerly hope that their son will become an official and make progress, but who knows that their son indulges in lust and even calls his father an old servant in front of his lover. Finally, he is accused of bigamy by two women. The development of this story on the screen is quite smooth, and the rhythm of the tone is also very peaceful.

In this film, the director has put a lot of effort into the handling and progress of the shots. For example, Xie Yunqing's two special shots behind the cigarette holder, and the close-ups of Gao Qianping, Yan Yuexian, and Gao Zhanfei's expressions are all techniques that should not be missed.

There are also many humorous places, such as Xie Yunqing's country bumpkin not knowing the doorbell and going to press it again and again. The life photos of college students, using dance magazines as extracurricular reading, climbing over the wall in the middle of the night, a fat man accidentally falling into a water tank, groping in the dark and accidentally stepping on a washbasin, and male students holding chairs to learn to dance are really funny, and inside, there is also a criticism of the corruption of modern education.

Among the actors, Xie Yunqing is the most successful. Yan Yongxian's facial photography is too dark, and the rest are competent.

Grand Premiere of "Rebirth Flower" 298

The plot of "Rebirth Flower" is more poignant and moving, and more twisted and regrettable than "Sister Flowers."

When Sister Flowers was released, many viewers sat in the theater, moved to tears. From the opening until Erbao rescued Dabao from prison and took her away, the audience was slightly relieved. But a disappointing feeling surged to their hearts: Dabao was taken away by Erbao, what happened afterwards? This meant they had to see the sequel to "Sister Flowers," "Rebirth Flower." Therefore, countless viewers longed for the premiere of "Rebirth Flower," which they had been eagerly anticipating. As a result, the entrance of the New Light Theater was crowded with traffic every day, and many viewers had a sense of looking at the ocean and sighing. Presumably, "Rebirth Flower" will set a new record and invigorate this silent Chinese film market.

"Flying Flower Village" is a Booming Success 299

The Art-China Film Company's singing blockbuster "Flying Flower Village", which is currently being screened at the Jin Cheng Grand Theater, is well received by society because everything depicted in the play is reality, and it has a sharp exposure of the sins caused by urban material civilization. It also has a profound depiction of the contradictory psychology of rural women who are tempted by material civilization, and since its opening on the 25th, the audience has been extremely enthusiastic, and the prosperity of the box office is comparable to the prosperity of "Woman" when it was screened in Shanghai.

Movie Novel

The Merry Widow (Part 3) 300

— Su Hua

The women waiting for him outside swarmed over and surrounded him. He laughed, sang, and kissed frantically; but who would know that this was Suria? She knew of his wildness at the door, and everyone inside greeted her as a dancer. A dancer who had just come in from outside asked her: "Are there any Americans tonight?" Another dancer named Marcia also told her some gossip about the dance hall. By chance, she saw Donner, who ran over to kiss her. They sat together. Marcia took out a very beautiful and precious garter from her leg and showed it to her, saying that Donner had given it to her. Suria took it over and saw that it said "From Jamie to Dorothy" inside. Suria thought that this Donner was really shocking. So she said her own name was Phoebe. When Donner moved closer to her, she said as if she were experienced: "It's not very good tonight, no Americans came. Are you a banker?" "No," Donner replied. She said disappointedly: "Ah! Aren't you? I'm only suitable for bankers. Do you understand what I mean?" Later, Donner ordered the waiter to open a private dining room on the second floor, room number seven. He tricked her into going in. A waiter went in with champagne and glasses, and then went out, and the door was closed. She looked at the room, which was simply furnished like a bedroom. This made her rush out again, almost knocking the waiter over. She had no choice but to go back. Donner softly said to her: "If you only like bankers, then the door of this room is not locked." Suria stared at him blankly. She understood his good intentions in her heart. She slowly walked to the door, her heart struggling with the question of whether to stay or leave. Donner saw this situation. He got up, locked the door, turned off the lights, and leaned in slightly. After waiting for a while, Donner opened the door and went in to see that she had not only not changed into her pajamas, but had also put on all her clothes. "What does this mean?" he asked in surprise. She pointed to the portrait of Napoleon hanging on the wall and said: "He failed at Waterloo because he attacked too early." Donner was so angry that he was speechless and embarrassed, and said angrily: "He failed at Waterloo, that's right, but what you're doing is too immoral." After he finished speaking, he opened the door and left angrily. He sat outside the door in a daze. Marcia came to push him, but he refused to move. The intoxicating music downstairs sounded, and the moving melody provoked everyone's emotions. Suria opened the door and walked closer to Donner. Looking at him gently, she said: "Let's dance." But he rudely refused. She had no choice but to go back to the room. She was disappointed, just like she was in her own garden before. In tears, she regretted coming here. The door suddenly opened, and Donner walked in, helped her up, and said softly: "Let's dance." At first, they danced as if they were strangers. But the soft music soon intoxicated them. Lips facing each other, eyes looking at each other. They had forgotten everything in the world. After a clear song, Suria felt involuntarily. Donner carefully held her and put her on the bed. Looking at her ecstatically, they had both received supreme comfort. When he leaned down to kiss her, Suria passionately asked: "Donner, do you love me?" He replied strangely: "Of course, why not?" She looked at him and carefully said again: "You have to understand, I'm asking if you really love me?" Donner happily replied: "Forever, until tomorrow." "What about after tomorrow?" she asked somewhat panic-stricken. "You're being a bit funny," he stopped kissing her, straightened up, and replied. She asked again: "Has anyone asked you this before?" "Not here," he replied lazily. She asked again: "You like the women here the most, don't you?" (To be continued)

Shen Bao Pictorial Special

(1) Smoke Screen Made of Sulfuric Acid 301

— (Far East News Agency)

Huang Bingfang, director of the Guangdong Provincial Sulfuric Acid Plant, recently used sulfuric acid to produce a thick smoke screen for military purposes. A public experiment was conducted at the Air Force Airport on the afternoon of the fourth of this month. Many important figures from the Political Committee attended the experiment. The results were extremely satisfactory. The picture shows the situation of the smoke screen being released.

(3) Anniversary of the October Revolution in Soviet Russia 302

The 17th anniversary of the October Revolution in Soviet Russia was celebrated with a military parade on Red Square in Moscow. The picture shows People's Commissar of Defense Voroshilov shaking hands with the military attaché of the Chinese Embassy in Russia before the inspection.

(4) Unique Parade 303

In the Moscow October Revolution anniversary parade, a model of a farmhouse made of rubber was carried through the city, which attracted much attention. This farmhouse was narrow and dark, and was the residence of farmers during the Tsarist era. With the success of the Five-Year Plan, rural areas have made significant progress, and this type of farmhouse is already a historical relic.

(8) Japan's Newly Built Streamlined Locomotive 305

— (Green)

This type of locomotive head was recently manufactured in Japan with a speed of eighty-five miles per hour and a traction force of 16,900 tons. Seven of them have been transported to Manchuria after being manufactured, and only one is running in Japan. Its ambition to manage Manchuria can be seen from this.

(9) Waiting for Relief 306

— (Yang Feng Studio)

After the disaster in Wangdian Township, Jiaxing, wailing can be heard everywhere and food supplies are running out. Bran and grass roots are used to fill hunger and the disaster is extremely tragic. The A-Xu All Zhejiang Disaster Relief Association specially sent Qi Qixian as the director of the relief investigation to the township to compile and investigate the disaster-stricken households waiting for relief, totaling more than 8,000 people. Each person was issued a bag of flour. The picture shows the disaster-stricken people holding tickets to receive relief after the compilation was completed.

Huangshan Photo Exhibition 307

To build famous scenery and prosper local areas, Zhejiang Construction has invited reporters from the Shanghai press to visit various scenic spots. The Huangshan Scenic Photography Exhibition initiated by Mr. Lang Jingshan and Bu Yu Xiang of the Huangshan Society is held after their return from Huangshan. The exhibition is open to the public at the Shanghai YMCA in Eight Immortals Bridge from the fifteenth to the seventeenth of this month. All the proceeds from the tickets will be donated to the YMCA for the Poor Children's Day to be given to poor children. It is especially a charity.

(4) Charity Football Match 308

— (Young)

The Wuchang Public Stadium launched a charity football match because the winter season is approaching and the victims need help. Various Chinese and foreign football teams in Wuhan enthusiastically participated. The picture shows one of the goals scored by our country's Ji Jian team against the French United team.

(5) The Down and Out Sai Jinhua in Beiping 309

Sai Jinhua's real name is Chuan Caiyun. She was a famous courtesan in the northern district. She married the top scholar Hong Jun at an early age and followed Hong on missions to various countries. During the Gengzi Rebellion with German General Waldersee, Waldersee was the commander of the Allied forces and led his troops into Beijing, where they looted and killed extremely brutally. At that time, Hong Jun had passed away and Sai resigned and returned to her old profession, changing her name to Sai Jinhua. She witnessed the tragedy and felt deeply saddened. She went to persuade Waldersee to issue strict orders to stop it, and many people were saved as a result. After the founding of the Republic of China, Sai was old and married Senator Wei Sihao. Not long after, Wei died and Sai was incompatible with Wei's family, so she drifted outside. Now Sai is over sixty years old and lives in a small alley in Beiping, number four, in a desolate state. These are her recent portraits.
